### [1] [Markov state models revisited: Principles and algorithms for unbiased observables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19452)
*David Aristof,Robert J. Webber,Daniel M. Zuckerman*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出用双转移矩阵框架替代传统单矩阵MSM，通过分别建模平衡动力学和源-汇循环动力学，在无限加权数据极限下获得任意固定滞后时间和粗粒化程度的无偏观测值，解决了传统MSM中模型偏差和长滞后时间导致短时程信息丢失的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统马尔可夫状态模型（MSM）使用单一转移矩阵，不得不选择较长的滞后时间来保证粗粒化动力学的马尔可夫性，这引入了可避免的模型偏差，并且掩盖了短时程动力学过程。

Method: 用两个转移矩阵——一个表示平衡动力学，另一个表示源-汇循环动力学——替代传统单矩阵框架，并针对匹配的动力学观测值选择正确的矩阵进行估计。

Result: 在无限、正确加权数据的极限下，可在任意固定滞后时间和任意固定粗粒化程度上获得无偏的粗粒化观测值。

Conclusion: 双转移矩阵方法能消除传统MSM中因长滞后时间选择带来的偏差，同时保留短时程动力学信息，为MSM分析提供了更灵活且无偏的框架。

Abstract: Markov state models (MSMs) have become ubiquitous tools for analyzing molecular dynamics (MD) simulations because of their simple, powerful premise: although complete MD sampling may be impossible, the MSM can "stitch together" transition probabilities derived from local sampling to provide a global picture of kinetics and mechanisms. In the standard MSM framework, the available MD data is organized into a single transition matrix, which is then used to estimate all observables at a lag time chosen so the coarse-grained dynamics are approximately Markovian. This approach leads to avoidable model bias and motivates long lag times that obscure short-timescale processes of interest. In contrast, this paper shows how to obtain unbiased coarse-grained observables at any fixed lag time and for any fixed coarse-graining in the limit of infinite, properly weighted data. The central idea is to replace the single-matrix framework with two transition matrices -- one representing equilibrium dynamics and another representing source-sink recycling dynamics -- and use the correct matrix or matrices to estimate the matched dynamical observables.

</details>


### [2] [Localization transitions of diffusion dynamics in physical networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19486)
*Jun Yamamoto,Ivan Bonamassa,Márton Pósfai*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了物理网络中的扩散过程，发现节点体积引入的局部停留时间会改变由拓扑驱动的拉普拉斯模态局域化，并揭示度-体积比作为关键无序参数，通过解析模型和实证网络展示了这一机制对特征模态的调控作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统网络扩散研究仅关注拓扑连接性，但物理网络中节点体积导致的停留时间会显著影响信息传播与弛豫过程，现有理论缺乏对这一物理异质性的系统性刻画。

Method: 构建了度-体积比作为无序参数的解析模型，求解该参数失谐对拉普拉斯谱的定性重构，并在实证网络中验证度-体积相关性如何将极端特征模态从拓扑选择的节点偏移。

Result: 度-体积比是调控拉普拉斯模态局域化的关键参数；物理异质性非平凡地重塑了网络动力学的无序景观，实现了特征丰富的局域化控制机制。

Conclusion: 物理性（节点体积）与拓扑性（度）的耦合构成网络扩散中更普适的局域化调控框架，为理解现实物理网络（如输运、通信系统）中的动力学行为提供了新视角。

Abstract: Network diffusion underlies many transport phenomena, with Laplacian modes setting how information spreads and relaxes. In physical networks, however, connectivity alone is not enough: node volumes introduce local dwell times that regulate how flow is stored before being propagated. Here we show that physical heterogeneity reshapes topology-driven localization, with the degree-volume ratio emerging as the relevant disorder parameter. We solve an analytical model in which ratio detuning qualitatively reorganizes the Laplacian spectrum, and demonstrate in empirical networks how degree-volume correlations shift extremal eigenmodes away from the nodes selected by topology alone. Our results reveal a general feature-rich-driven mechanism for localization control, showing that physicality non-trivially reshapes the disorder landscape governing network dynamics.

</details>


### [3] [Random walks in Dirichlet random environment in dimension $d+1$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20279)
*Guillaume Barraquand,Alexander K. Hartmann,Pierre Le Doussal*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟研究了1、2、3维空间中具有Dirichlet分布转移概率的离散随机游走模型，验证了其在d=1和d=2时与KPZ增长的一致性，在d=3时发现了弱/强无序相变，并精确计算了热平均方差的样本间波动及其与极端扩散系数的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机游走在时变随机环境中的非典型行为近年来被发现与Kardar-Parisi-Zhang（KPZ）增长相关。尽管d=1维度的这一联系已得到很好理解，但在更高维度（d>1）中仍需进一步探索。

Method: 采用数值模拟方法，研究了一种具有Dirichlet分布转移概率的离散模型（d=1可积模型的推广），该模型具有显式的乘积形式平稳测度。通过分析从原点到位置x在时间t的点到点概率的对数方差增长，并与KPZ增长预测进行比较。

Result: d=1和d=2维度下，点到点概率对数方差增长与KPZ增长兼容；d=3维度下，随着角度|x|/t增加观察到相变。弱无序相中点到点概率呈重尾分布，强无序相中其对数的累积量随时间增长。基于精确二阶矩计算给出了下界。精确计算了热平均⟨x⟩²的样本间方差，并发现其与极端扩散系数相关。

Conclusion: 该模型为研究高维随机环境中KPZ增长提供了有效框架，特别是在d=3中揭示了弱无序到强无序的相变行为，并建立了热平均方差与极端扩散系数之间的联系。

Abstract: The atypical behaviour of random walks in time-dependent random environment was recently related to Kardar-Parisi-Zhang (KPZ) growth. While this is now well-understood in spatial dimension $d=1$, further efforts are necessary to better understand these connections in dimensions $d>1$. In this paper, we study this problem numerically for $d=1, 2$ and $3$, focusing on a discrete model with Dirichlet distributed transition probabilities. This model is a generalization of an integrable model in $d=1$, and it has the advantage of admitting an explicit, product-form, stationary measure. We verify that the growth of the variance of the logarithm of point-to-point probabilities, namely from the origin to position $x$ in time $t$, is compatible with KPZ growth in dimension $d=1$ and $d=2$. In spatial dimension $d=3$, we confirm the existence of a phase transition as the angle $\vert x\vert /t$ increases and we obtain a lower bound based on an exact second moment calculation. We find that in the weak disorder phase the point-to-point probability acquires a heavy tailed distribution, and that in the strong disorder phase the cumulants of its logarithm grow with time. Further, we show that for this model, we can compute exactly the sample to sample variance of the thermal average $\overline{ \langle x \rangle^2}$ and that it is related to the extreme diffusion coefficient introduced recently.

</details>


### [4] [Weakly Nonlinear Dynamics of Unstable Modes in Jammed Amorphous Solids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19818)
*Kota Noto,Harukuni Ikeda,Kuniyasu Saitoh,Hisao Hayakawa*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过构建含波数调制的广义Hessian矩阵，研究非晶固体在堵塞态下的结构演化。该广义公式通过傅里叶扩展捕捉线性不稳定模式，发现不稳定本征模的激发会导致与初始扰动无关的结构重排，并推导了类似朗道方程的弱非线性振幅方程来描述不稳定模式的增长与饱和。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Hessian矩阵仅适用于力学稳定态，无法研究非晶固体在力学不稳定区域的响应。本文旨在通过推广Hessian矩阵，纳入波数空间调制，从而捕捉不稳定模式并理解由此引发的结构重排机制。

Method: 构建广义Hessian矩阵（在传统Hessian基础上通过波数进行傅里叶扩展）；通过数值模拟激发不稳定本征模，观察结构重排；推导弱非线性振幅方程（类比Landau方程）描述不稳定模式的增长与饱和过程。

Result: 不稳定本征模的激发会导致结构重排，且该重排与初始微扰方式无关；推导出的弱非线性振幅方程能够有效描述不稳定模式的演化行为。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一种理解非晶固体中失稳驱动构型变化的通用框架，拓展了传统Hessian分析方法的适用范围。

Abstract: We investigate the structural evolution in jammed amorphous solids by analyzing the eigenmodes of a generalized Hessian matrix that incorporates spatial modulation via wave numbers. Unlike the conventional Hessian, this generalized formulation captures linearly unstable modes through a Fourier-based extension of the Hessian matrix, enabling us to study responses beyond the mechanically stable regime. We demonstrate that the excitation of unstable eigenmodes leads to structural rearrangements independent of the initial perturbation by the simulation. Furthermore, we derive a weakly nonlinear amplitude equation to describe the growth and saturation of these unstable modes, analogous to the Landau equation. Our framework provides a pathway to understand instability-driven configuration changes in disordered solids.

</details>


### [5] [Motility destabilizes an absorbing-state flock](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20034)
*Narayan Dutt Sharma,Subroto Mukerjee,Chandan Dasgupta,Sriram Ramaswamy*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出一个一维晶格模型，在非运动极限下呈现吸收铁磁态，而引入偏向运动（活性）后会 destabilize 这些吸收态，导致系统随对齐强度减弱从有序 flock 向无序态转变。有限尺寸标度分析表明连续相变，临界指数满足一维超标度关系，定量证明了活性诱导的无序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通常认为运动（活性）能促进多体系统中的有序，但本文旨在展示活性反而可以诱导无序，通过设计一个模型来定量研究这一反直觉现象。

Method: 构建一维晶格模型，在非运动极限下系统存在吸收铁磁态；通过引入偏向运动（活性）来破坏这些有序态，并改变对齐强度观察系统行为。采用有限尺寸标度分析物理量，计算临界指数并检验超标度关系。

Result: 活性 destabilize 了吸收有序态，系统随着对齐强度减弱经历从有序 flock 到无序态的连续相变；有限尺寸标度分析得到的临界指数满足一维超标度关系。

Conclusion: 活性并不总是促进有序，在本模型中它诱导了无序；该连续相变及其临界行为在定量上得到了验证。

Abstract: Activity, when it takes the form of motility, is generally seen to promote order in many-body systems. Here we present a one-dimensional lattice model that, in the non-motile limit, exhibits absorbing ferromagnetic states. When activity is introduced through biased motility, these absorbing state are destabilised and the system instead undergoes a transition from an ordered flock to a disordered state as the alignment strength is decreased. A finite-size scaling analysis of physical quantities reveals a continuous transition with critical exponents satisfying the hyperscaling relation in one dimension, providing quantitative evidence for the activity-induced disorder.

</details>


### [6] [Logarithmic scaling correction in quench dynamics of the J1-J2 Potts model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20081)
*Kun Li,Wanzhou Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了J1-J2反铁磁Potts模型在热淬火动力学中的Kibble-Zurek机制标度行为，发现淬火终止于准长程有序（QLRO）相时，过剩能量密度呈现对数修正的KZM标度；而终止于长程有序（LRO）相时，则遵循传统幂律标度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清在具有两个连续拓扑相变的离散自旋系统中，热淬火动力学是否会出现对数标度修正，填补KZM在J1-J2 Potts模型中的研究空白。

Method: 构建J1-J2反铁磁Potts模型的平衡相图，基于顺磁相、QLRO相、LRO相和零温基态的温度区间，设计四种不同温度间隔的淬火协议，通过数值模拟分析过剩能量密度的标度行为。

Result: 淬火终止于QLRO相时，过剩能量密度呈现对数修正的KZM标度，与2D XY模型的动力学普适类一致；淬火终止于LRO相（包括有限温和零温协议）时，遵循传统幂律标度。

Conclusion: 清晰地揭示了J1-J2 Potts模型的特征标度修正，为未来通过光子模拟平台实验研究KZM提供了理论指导。

Abstract: In conventional quench dynamics governed by the Kibble-Zurek mechanism (KZM), the defect density generally decays as a pure power law of the quench rate. However, the KZM scaling of the two-dimensional (2D) XY model with topological phase transitions features prominent logarithmic corrections. Nevertheless, it remains unclear whether such logarithmic scaling corrections emerge in discrete-spin systems that host two successive topological phase transitions under thermal quenches. This work investigates the J1-J2 antiferromagnetic Potts model and constructs its equilibrium phase diagram. Based on the temperature ranges of the paramagnetic phase, quasi-long-range ordered (QLRO) phase, long-range ordered phase, and zero-temperature ground state, we design four quench protocols with distinct temperature intervals. Our results demonstrate that quenches terminating in the QLRO phase exhibit logarithmically corrected KZM scaling of the excess energy density, consistent with the dynamical universality class of the 2D XY model. In contrast, quenches ending in the LRO phase, including both finite-temperature and zero-temperature protocols, follow conventional power-law scaling. Our results clearly uncover the characteristic scaling corrections of the J1-J2 Potts model and offer theoretical guidance for future experimental investigations of KZM via photonic simulation platforms.

</details>


### [7] [Derivation of the Boltzmann equation with no "molecular chaos"-type approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20134)
*Victor F. Los*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文从 Liouville 方程出发，在不使用“分子混沌”假设的情况下，推导出了 N 粒子系统中 s 粒子分布函数 F_s(t) 的完全闭合演化方程。通过引入特殊的投影算子，将含初始关联项的非齐次 Nakajima-Zwanzig 广义主方程转化为齐次形式。在粒子密度 n 的线性近似下，导出了单粒子和双粒子分布函数的方程，并证明初始关联项在大时间尺度下消失，从而得到线性 Boltzmann 方程，该方程在特定条件下可表示为非线性 Boltzmann 方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决从 Liouville 方程推导 s 粒子分布函数 F_s(t) 完全闭合演化方程的问题，避免使用“分子混沌”类近似，并正确处理初始关联的影响。

Method: 利用特殊的投影算子将含初始关联项的非齐次 Nakajima-Zwanzig 广义主方程转化为齐次方程；然后在粒子密度 n 的线性近似下对方程进行简化，推导出 F_1(t) 和 F_2(t) 的方程。

Result: 在密度线性近似下，F_1(t) 方程中描述初始关联影响的项在时间尺度 t ~ t_rel >> t_cor 下消失，得到线性 Boltzmann 方程；在 t_cor << t << t_rel 区间可表示为非线性 Boltzmann 方程；当 t_rel → ∞（平均自由程 l → ∞）时，Boltzmann 方程对所有有限时间 t >> t_cor 成立。

Conclusion: 成功在不使用分子混沌假设的情况下，从第一性原理推导出闭合的动力学方程，并阐明了初始关联在动力学演化中的作用及其在大时间尺度下的消退机制，为 Boltzmann 方程的严格推导提供了新的途径。

Abstract: The paper resolves the problem of the derivation of a completely closed evolution equation for $s$-particle distribution function $F_s(t)$ ($s \le N$) from the Liouville equation for $N \gg 1$-particle distribution function $F_N(t)$ with arbitrary initial condition $F_N(0)$ and without any use of the "molecular chaos" type approximation. The initial correlations are accounted for in this equation in the kernel governing the evolution of $F_s(t)$ via the special projection operator which exactly transforms the inhomogeneous Nakajima-Zwanzig Generalized Master Equation (GME) with an irrelevant initial condition term into the homogenous one. This equation is further simplified by presenting its kernel in the linear in the particles' density $n$ approximation. In this approximation the equations for one-particle $F_1(t)$ and two-particle $F_2(t)$ distribution functions are derived. It is shown that the terms describing the influence of initial correlations in the equation for $F_1(t)$ disappear at the large timescale $t \sim t_{\text{rel}} \gg t_{\text{cor}}$ ($t_{\text{cor}}$ is a short correlation time as compared to a relaxation time $t_{\text{rel}}$ of $F_1(t)$) resulting in the linear Boltzmann equation. This equation can be presented as the nonlinear Boltzmann equation in the time interval $t_{\text{cor}} \ll t \ll t_{\text{rel}}$. At $t_{\text{rel}} \to \infty$ (mean free path $l \to \infty$) the Boltzmann equation holds for all finite times $t \gg t_{\text{cor}}$.

</details>


### [8] [Optimal Finite-Time Control of Nonreciprocal Brownian Dimers: Thermodynamic Anomaly and Multiple Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20420)
*Ruicheng Bao*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文精确求解了两个非互易相互作用的布朗粒子在简谐势阱驱动下的有限时间热力学最优控制问题。研究发现存在一个临界时间，超过该时间可提取功和下界为负无穷，即输出功率无界；物理正则化（有限势阱范围、力饱和）将此异常转化为最优协议相变，包括一级类跃变和二级连续转变，并揭示了多重有限时间转变的新现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究非互易相互作用（主动力）在有限时间热力学最优控制中的角色，特别是这种内部主动力如何耦合两个控制通道（质心和间距），以及是否会导致超出传统热力学极限的奇异行为。

Method: 对两个非互易耦合的布朗粒子体系进行精确求解，控制器同时操控两个简谐势阱的质心和间距。分别分析无约束情况、有限势阱范围（硬约束）以及力饱和（软约束）下的最优协议。

Result: 1）最优协议呈振荡形式，即使目标间距不变也需主动打开二聚体；2）存在临界时间，超过后外部功下界为负无穷，即提取功和输出功率无界；3）有限势阱范围导致一级相变（零协议突变为最大范围协议），力饱和导致二级连续转变；4）有限范围下最优协议可发生多次有限时间转变，功-时长曲线呈现多个扭结。

Conclusion: 非互易相互作用在有限时间控制中可产生反常的热力学行为（功下界发散），物理正则化不仅消除了这一反常，还引入了新的最优协议相变类型，丰富了有限时间热力学控制理论。

Abstract: We solve exactly a finite-time thermodynamic optimal control problem for two nonreciprocally interacting Brownian particles translated by two harmonic traps. The controller manipulates both the center and separation of the pair. Nonreciprocal interactions generate an internal active force that couples these two channels. The optimal protocol is oscillatory, deliberately opens the dimer even when the target separation is unchanged, and can extract work during transport. A central finding is a finite critical time beyond which the external-work infimum is $-\infty$: at any prescribed duration beyond this threshold, both extractable work and output power are unbounded. Physical regularizations such as finite trap range and force saturation restore a finite optimum and convert the anomaly into optimal-protocol transitions: in the zero-target case, a hard finite range produces a first-order-like jump from the zero protocol to a maximum-range protocol, whereas smooth force saturation gives a continuous, second-order-like onset. Under finite-range constraints, the optimal protocol can further undergo multiple finite-time transitions, producing multiple work-duration kinks with no qualitative analog in prior studies.

</details>


### [9] [Stable valleys in the glassy landscape of a low-density parity-check (LDPC) code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20421)
*Grace M. Sommers,David A. Huse*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究基于扩展图定义的经典LDPC码所对应的统计力学模型，发现其在低温下存在多种稳定且不匹配的能谷，且微正则系综与正则系综在某些能谷中不等价。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典LDPC码是构建优良量子LDPC码的基础，同时其自身定义了有趣的统计力学模型——包含无淬火随机性或阻挫的自旋玻璃序。作者希望探究这类系统中低温下能谷结构的性质以及不同系综之间的等价性问题。

Method: 采用局部树状扩展图上的经典LDPC码作为案例，利用其局部树状性质进行树上的递归技术分析，研究施加不同边界条件在低温下诱发的稳定、不匹配能谷。同时在封闭有限图上进行数值研究，比较微正则系综与正则系综在不同能谷中的行为。

Result: 发现了多种稳定且互不匹配的能谷，由不同边界条件在低温下诱导产生。数值结果表明，在某些能谷中，微正则系综与正则系综不等价。

Conclusion: 局部树状扩展图上的经典LDPC码呈现出丰富的能谷结构，且系综不等价现象出现，这加深了对无淬火随机性自旋玻璃序的理解，也为量子LDPC码的物理性质提供了启示。

Abstract: Classical low-density parity-check (cLDPC) codes defined on expander graphs are a fundamental ingredient in the construction of good quantum LDPC codes, a recent milestone in quantum error correction. They also define interesting statistical mechanics models in their own right, as they include examples of spin glass order without quenched randomness or frustration. We investigate this via a case study of a cLDPC code on a locally tree-like expander graph. Recursive techniques on trees, made possible by the locally tree-like property, probe a menagerie of stable, incongruent valleys induced by imposing different boundary conditions at low temperature. A complementary numerical study of the valleys on closed finite graphs reveals the inequivalence of the microcanonical and canonical ensemble for certain valleys.

</details>

# math.AP [[Back]](#toc)

### [10] [Uniform a priori estimates for slightly subcritical fractional problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19480)
*Juan-Carlos Felipe-Navarro,Rosa Pardo*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了分数阶半线性Dirichlet问题中正弱解的一致L∞先验有界性，针对略超线性非线性项f(t)=t^q L(t)（其中q达到临界指数且L为慢变函数），通过引入一个渐近结构条件lim_{t→∞} t|L'(t)|/L^{N/(2s)}(t)=∞，防止了气泡集中现象，从而在临界情形下建立了全局一致有界性，显著扩展了已知非线性函数的类别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在分数阶半线性Dirichlet问题中，对于略超线性非线性项，临界指数情形（q=(N+2s)/(N-2s)）下可能形成气泡集中（bubbling profiles），使得一致L∞估计极具挑战性。现有结果仅覆盖严格次临界情形（q<(N+2s)/(N-2s)），而临界情形缺乏统一的先验有界性理论。本文旨在填补这一空白，识别出能够阻止质量集中发生的结构条件。

Method: 本文从分析角度出发，考察略超线性非线性项f(t)=t^q L(t)中慢变函数L(t)的渐近行为，提出并验证了条件 lim_{t→∞} t|L'(t)|/L^{N/(2s)}(t)=∞ 作为防止质量集中的渐近屏障。在此条件下，利用该结构条件对慢变扰动的限制，结合分数阶拉普拉斯算子的相关分析工具，推导出正弱解的一致L∞界。

Result: 建立了在临界指数情形下正弱解的全局一致L∞(Ω)有界性，该结果适用于一类更广泛的非线性函数（即满足所提结构条件的慢变扰动），显著扩充了已知可建立此类估计的非线性函数类别。

Conclusion: 所提出的渐近结构条件有效阻断了临界情形下可能形成的质量集中现象，从而在更广泛的非线性函数类中获得了分数阶半线性Dirichlet问题正弱解的一致先验有界性。这为理解分数阶非线性椭圆方程中解的正则性和紧性提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We study the uniform $L^\infty(Ω)$ a priori boundedness of positive weak solutions to the fractional semilinear Dirichlet problem $(-Δ)^s u = f(u)$ in a bounded, convex, $C^{1,1}$ domain $Ω\subset \mathbb{R}^N$ with homogeneous exterior condition $u\equiv 0$ in $\mathbb{R}^N\setminusΩ$. We consider slightly superlinear nonlinearities of the form $f(t) = t^q L(t)$, where $1 \le q \le \frac{N+2s}{N-2s}$ and $L$ is a slowly varying function. Although uniform estimates are well-established in the strictly subcritical regime $q < \frac{N+2s}{N-2s}$, the slightly subcritical case, $q = \frac{N+2s}{N-2s}$, is highly challenging due to the potential formation of bubbling profiles.
  In this work, we isolate a structural condition on the slowly varying perturbation, namely $$ \lim_{t \to \infty} \frac{t \, |L'(t)|}{L^{\frac{N}{2s}}(t)} = \infty, $$ which acts as an asymptotic barrier that prevents mass concentration. Under this assumption, we establish global uniform $L^\infty(Ω)$ bounds for positive solutions, significantly expanding the class of known nonlinearities for which such estimates hold.

</details>


### [11] [Recovery of nonlinearity from the modified scattering map for cubic NLS with a repulsive delta potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19613)
*Mengyi Xie*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究一维三次非线性薛定谔方程（带排斥δ势和局部非均匀系数），证明了小数据修正散射并构造了向量值修正散射映射，该映射能同时恢复δ势强度（Lipschitz稳定）和非均匀系数（Hölder稳定），是首个在外势下修正散射映射的恢复与稳定性结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有修正散射理论多针对无外势情形，而实际物理系统中外势（如δ势）和非均匀系数普遍存在。本文旨在探索如何从修正散射映射中同时恢复这两类参数，填补外势下修正散射反问题研究的空白。

Method: 采用小数据修正散射分析方法，考虑排斥δ势和局部非均匀系数对非线性薛定谔方程的影响。通过构造向量值修正散射映射，捕捉频率ξ和-ξ之间由点相互作用引起的耦合效应，并分别建立δ势强度和非均匀系数的稳定性估计。

Result: 证明了修正散射映射能够同时确定δ势强度（Lipschitz稳定性）和非均匀系数（Hölder稳定性），且这是首次在外势存在的情况下获得修正散射映射的恢复与稳定性结果。

Conclusion: 本文建立了外势下修正散射反问题的首个恢复与稳定性理论，为通过散射数据反演外势和非均匀系数提供了理论基础，拓展了修正散射方法的应用范围。

Abstract: We study the one-dimensional cubic nonlinear Schrödinger equation with a repulsive delta potential and a localized inhomogeneous coefficient. We prove small-data modified scattering and construct the associated vector-valued modified scattering map, whose two components encode the coupling of the frequencies $ξ$ and $-ξ$ induced by the point interaction. We show that this map determines both the strength of the delta potential and the inhomogeneous coefficient. Quantitatively, the delta strength is recovered with Lipschitz stability, while the inhomogeneous coefficients satisfy a Hölder stability estimate. To our knowledge, these are the first recovery and stability results for a modified scattering map in the presence of an external potential.

</details>


### [12] [Classification of minimizing solutions to a two-dimensional Allen-Cahn system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19671)
*Zhiyuan Geng*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有D₃不变三阱势能的Allen-Cahn泛函的全体极小解，给出了完整分类。特别地，当解在无穷远处具有三叉结结构时，解必须显式地表示为uₙ(𝐱)=∑ᵢ₌₁³ (e^{√2 a_i·𝐱}/∑ⱼ₌₁³ e^{√2 a_j·𝐱}) a_i（在平移和正交坐标变换意义下）。同时还证明了D₃等变类中的极小化解恰好就是uₙ。关键工具是源于势能W特殊代数结构的校准恒等式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对具有三阱势能的Allen-Cahn泛函，其极小解在无穷远处可能呈现三叉结结构（triple-junction），这是一种典型的奇异界面模式。理解这类解的完整分类对于相场模型中的多相界面理论具有重要意义。现有工作对双阱势（标量场）的极小解已有较完整刻画，但对三阱势（向量场）的全局极小解分类尚不完善，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 1) 利用势能W的D₃对称性和特殊代数结构，推导出一个校准恒等式（calibration identity）；2) 基于该恒等式建立能量下界估计，并借助匹配渐近分析，证明极小解在无穷远处的渐近行为必须符合三叉结结构；3) 通过刚性分析（rigidity argument）证明，在平移和正交变换下，全体极小解唯一地由显式公式uₙ给出；4) 对D₃等变类中的极小化问题，利用对称性进一步简化，证明其解恰好就是uₙ。

Result: 1) 得到了具有D₃不变三阱势的Allen-Cahn泛函全体极小解的完整分类；2) 当极小解在无穷远处呈现三叉结结构时，解在平移和正交坐标变换下具有唯一的显式解析形式uₙ；3) D₃等变极小化解必等于uₙ。

Conclusion: 基于势能W的代数结构导出的校准恒等式，成功完成了对三阱Allen-Cahn极小解的完全分类。这为多相界面问题中的极小构型刻画提供了严格的数学框架，并揭示了显式解uₙ在该类问题中的普遍性。

Abstract: We study bounded entire solutions $u:\mathbb{R}^2\to \mathbb{R}^2$ that minimize the Allen-Cahn functional
  \begin{equation*}
  J(u,Ω)=\int_Ω\left(\frac12 |\nabla u|^2+W(u)\right)\,d\mathbf{x},
  \end{equation*}
  with the $D_3$-invariant triple-well potential
  \begin{equation*}
  W(u_1,u_2)=|u|^4+2u_1u_2^2-\frac23 u_1^3-|u|^2+\frac23.
  \end{equation*}
  We obtain a complete classification of entire minimizing solutions. In particular, when $u$ has a triple-junction structure at infinity, up to translation and orthogonal change of coordinates, $u$ has the explicit profile
  \begin{equation*}
  u_*(\mathbf{x})=\sum_{i=1}^3 \frac{e^{\sqrt2 a_i\cdot \mathbf{x}}}{\sum_{j=1}^3 e^{\sqrt2 a_j\cdot \mathbf{x}}}a_i.
  \end{equation*}
  We also demonstrate that the solutions obtained by minimizing within the $D_3$-equivariant class coincide with $u_*$. The key ingredient is a calibration identity arising from the special algebraic structure of $W$.

</details>


### [13] [On the characterization of polyharmonic functions through iterated means](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19684)
*Fernando Charro,Catherine Lebiedzik,Md Nurul Raihen*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文引入了一个由迭代均值线性组合构成的无穷均值公式族（精确与渐近形式），证明该族公式能刻画有限阶实值多调和函数，并通过简单代数条件按多调和阶数划分等价类。核心结果包括：满足该族中均值性质的局部可积函数必然是光滑的多调和函数（均值性质的强逆命题），以及无论精确还是渐近形式，满足均值性质的局部可积函数都是光滑的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统均值性质仅能刻画调和函数（零阶多调和），而高阶多调和函数缺乏类似的特征刻画。本文旨在建立一套统一的、可区分不同阶数多调和函数的均值公式体系，并回答逆问题：满足广义均值性质的函数是否自动具有多调和性与光滑性。

Method: 构造一个由迭代均值线性组合构成的无穷均值公式族，通过引入代数条件对公式按多调和阶数分类。利用势论与分布理论，证明满足该族中任一均值性质的局部可积函数必然满足对应的多调和方程，并证明其无穷可微性。

Result: 1. 该均值公式族中的每个公式精准刻画对应阶数的多调和函数；2. 满足族中任一均值性质的局部可积函数一定是光滑的多调和函数（强逆命题）；3. 无论精确均值性质还是渐近均值性质，均能推出函数的光滑性。

Conclusion: 建立了多调和函数的完整均值特征体系，将经典的调和函数均值性质推广到了任意阶多调和情形，同时证明了该特征刻画在正则性方面的强大性质——均值性质本身就蕴含光滑性，无需额外假设。

Abstract: We introduce an infinite family of mean-value formulas (exact and asymptotic) given in terms of linear combinations of iterated means. We prove that the mean-value formulas in this family characterize real-valued polyharmonic functions of finite order, and that a simple algebraic condition partitions the family into equivalence classes according to the order of polyharmonicity. Our key results include strong converses to the mean-value properties -- locally integrable functions satisfying a mean-value property in the family are polyharmonic -- and a regularity result -- locally integrable functions satisfying a mean-value property in the family, whether exact or asymptotic, are smooth.

</details>


### [14] [Self-Similar Solutions of the Two-Dimensional Incompressible Euler Equation from Large Initial Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19700)
*Hyungjun Choi*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文针对二维不可压缩欧拉方程，在初始速度场为C^1、无散且(-a)-齐次（其中1/3<a<1）的条件下，构造了向前自相似解，无需小量或符号假设，通过消失耗散极限方法实现，关键是在临界Lorentz空间中获得了一致估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究具有奇异性或非正则初始数据的欧拉方程解的适定性，特别是构造具有齐次性初始数据的自相似解，并克服无小量假设的困难。

Method: 采用消失耗散极限方法：先考虑hypodissipative（亚耗散）正则化系统，构造自相似剖面估计，再令耗散参数趋于零，关键工具是临界Lorentz空间L^{2/(1+a),∞}中的一致估计。

Result: 成功构造了二维欧拉方程的向前自相似解，解具有局部有限能量，速度梯度位于L^∞_t L^{2/(1+a),∞}_x空间，速度在L^2_loc中连续，涡度在初始时刻弱-*收敛于L^{2/(1+a),∞}。

Conclusion: 该工作证明了在较弱的正则性条件下（无需小量或符号条件），欧拉方程仍存在自相似解，推广了经典结果，并为研究奇异解提供了新工具。

Abstract: Let $\frac{1}{3}<a<1$ and let $u_0$ be a $C^1$, divergence-free, $(-a)$-homogeneous vector field on $\mathbb{R}^2\setminus\{0\}$. We construct a forward-in-time self-similar solution of the two-dimensional incompressible Euler equations, \[ u(t,x)=t^{-\frac{a}{1+a}} U\left(\frac{x}{t^{{\frac{1}{1+a}}}}\right), \] with initial datum $u_0$. No smallness or sign assumption is imposed on the initial datum. The construction is a vanishing-dissipation limit of the hypodissipative self-similar profiles. The key is a vorticity profile estimate, uniform in the dissipation parameter, in the critical Lorentz space $L^{\frac{2}{1+a},\infty}(\mathbb{R}^2)$.
  The resulting Euler solution $u$ has locally finite energy and $\nabla u \in L^\infty_t L^{\frac{2}{1+a},\infty}_x$. Indeed, the velocity is continuous in $L^2_{\text{loc}}$, and the vorticity converges weak-* in $L^{\frac{2}{1+a},\infty}$ at the initial time.

</details>


### [15] [Global uniform regularity and large time behavior of solutions to three dimensional compressible MHD equations with vanishing vertical magnetic resistivity in half space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19710)
*Song Gao,Jiahong Wu,Feng Xie*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了三维可压缩磁流体动力学(MHD)方程在垂直磁阻率趋于零时的全局正则性与大时间行为，建立了与ε无关的一致正则性估计，证明了极限收敛性，并推导了H¹衰减率和ε^{1/4}阶的L²收敛速率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立三维可压缩MHD方程在垂直磁阻率消失时的全局正则性和大时间行为理论，克服边界层带来的分析困难，严格刻画从耗散系统到无垂直磁阻率系统的极限过程。

Method: 利用各向异性Sobolev不等式和精细估计建立与ε无关的一致正则性估计；通过线性化算子的半群分析和一致能量估计推导H¹衰减率；结合正则性与衰减结果证明极限过程的L²收敛速率。

Result: 获得了全局一致正则性估计；证明了ε→0时收敛到无垂直磁阻率的MHD系统；得到了H¹(R³₊)空间的衰减率（较极限系统更慢）；证明了时间一致的ε^{1/4}阶L²收敛速率。

Conclusion: 完成了对垂直磁阻率消失极限过程的严格数学分析，揭示了边界层导致衰减率下降的机制，并为可压缩MHD方程奇异极限问题提供了新的分析框架。

Abstract: This paper aims to establish the global regularity and large time behavior of solutions to the three-dimensional (3D) compressible magnetohydrodynamics (MHD) equations with vanishing vertical magnetic resistivity in the upper half-space with no-slip boundary condition on velocity and perfectly conducting boundary condition on magnetic field. By exploiting anisotropic Sobolev inequalities and elaborated estimates, we are able to achieve global-in-time uniform regularity estimates of solutions, which are independent of small vertical resistivity coefficient $\varepsilon$. These uniform global regularity estimates allow us to pass to the limit as \(\varepsilon \to 0\) and obtain the convergence to the corresponding MHD system without vertical magnetic resistivity globally in time. Moreover, the $H^{1}\left(\mathbb{R}_{+}^{3}\right)$ decay rates of solutions to the original system are also derived based on the detailed analysis on semigroup of the related linearized operator in half space and the uniform energy estimates achieved. In contrast to the decay estimates for the limit system obtained by Gao and Xie \cite{JDE}, the present decay estimate exhibits a slower rate, attributable to the absence of higher-order normal derivative estimates, which results from the occurrence of boundary layers. Finally, we combine both sets of regularity and decay results to rigorously prove an explicit time-uniform $L^2$ convergence rate of order $\varepsilon^{\frac{1}{4}}$ for the vanishing vertical magnetic resistivity limit process.

</details>


### [16] [Regularity and Decay for Navier-Slip Fluid-Structure Interaction in Exterior Domains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19736)
*Buma Jin Jin*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了在Navier滑移边界条件下，浸没于不可压缩粘性流体中的球形刚体的线性化运动，利用球体的几何正则性建立了流体-结构算子的强$L^q$正则性、有界解析性及尖锐$L^q-L^r$估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无滑移边界条件下的半群正则性和衰减估计已得到充分理解，但在滑移边界条件下，此类结果仅限于有界区域。本文旨在填补全空间背景下滑移边界条件流体-结构耦合问题的理论空白。

Method: 通过利用球体的几何正则性（对称性），对Navier滑移边界条件下的流体-结构耦合算子进行谱分析和半群方法研究，建立强$L^q$-正则性、有界解析性以及尖锐的$L^q-L^r$估计。

Result: 建立了该流体-结构算子的强$L^q$正则性、有界解析性及尖锐的$L^q-L^r$时空估计。

Conclusion: 所得结果为构建相应非线性系统的强$W^{2,1}_q$解和Kato型解提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We study the linearized motion of a spherical rigid body immersed in an incompressible viscous fluid occupying the whole space, under Navier slip boundary conditions with friction. While semigroup regularity and decay estimates are well understood for the no-slip case, such results have been limited to bounded domains in the slip setting. By exploiting the geometric regularity of the sphere, we establish strong $L^q$-regularity, bounded analyticity, and sharp $ L^q-L^r$ estimates for the corresponding fluid-structure operator. These results would provide a foundation for constructing strong $W^{2,1}_q$ solutions and Kato-type solutions to the corresponding nonlinear system.

### [17] [Ellipsoidal characterization of neutral inclusions for imperfect bonding of high-conductivity type](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19791)
*Junyong Eom,Shota Fukushima,Yong-Gwan Ji,Hyeonbae Kang,Xiaofei Li,Shigeru Sakaguchi*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文证明了若一个高传导型不完全粘结的夹杂物对所有均匀场呈中性，则该夹杂物必为椭圆或椭球体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已知椭圆和椭球体可通过在边界上引入适当的不完全粘结系数来对所有均匀场呈中性，但该几何形状是否为必要条件尚不明确。本文旨在证明其逆命题。

Method: 将中性条件转化为边界曲面上某个微分方程解的存在性问题，进而将中性条件转换为刻画椭圆和椭球体的代数边界恒等式，从而完成证明。

Result: 证明了高传导型不完全粘结夹杂物若对所有均匀场呈中性，则其形状必为椭圆（二维）或椭球体（三维）。

Conclusion: 椭圆和椭球体是高传导型不完全粘结中性夹杂物的唯一可能形状，完善了该类中性夹杂物的几何表征理论。

Abstract: This paper concerns neutral inclusions for imperfect bonding of high-conductivity type. An inclusion, which is a bounded domain, is said to be of imperfect bonding of high-conductivity type if the flux is discontinuous along its boundary while the potential is continuous. The inclusion is neutral to a uniform field if the presence of the inclusion does not perturb the field outside the inclusion. It is known that ellipses and ellipsoids can be neutral to all uniform fields by introducing a proper imperfect bonding coefficient on boundaries. The purpose of this paper is to prove the converse. We prove that if an inclusion of imperfect bonding of high-conductivity type is neutral to all uniform fields, then it is an ellipse or an ellipsoid. The neutrality condition is given by existence of the solution to a certain differential equation on the boundary surface and the main result is proved by converting the neutrality condition into an algebraic boundary identity characterizing ellipses and ellipsoids.

</details>


### [18] [Simultaneous Recovery of the Initial Source and Sound Speed for the Wave Equation under a Constitutive Constraint](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19799)
*Amir Moradifam*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究从单一边界测量同时反演波动方程的初始源和声速。通过引入两个未知量之间的本构关系（源自共同底层材料），在定量非退化条件下将耦合反问题简化为单个逆源问题，并利用Stefanov-Uhlmann的微局部和Carleman框架，在严格凸叶状结构和测地线可见性等几何条件下，建立了全局唯一性和Lipschitz稳定性，同时获得了局部可见区域的唯一性和稳定性结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 波动方程中初始源和声速的单独反演在合适几何假设下已有成熟理解，但两者的同时反演在一般情况下仍然开放，且线性化问题的固有不稳定性进一步阻碍了稳定恢复。因此，需要探索在何种条件下可以实现同时反演的唯一性和稳定性。

Method: 假设两个未知量通过一个源自共同底层材料的本构关系耦合。在定量非退化条件（受校准材料状态启发）下，将耦合反问题简化为单一逆源问题。随后应用Stefanov和Uhlmann的微局部和Carleman框架，在严格凸叶状结构和测地线可见性等几何条件下进行分析。

Result: 建立了全局唯一性和Lipschitz稳定性；同时获得部分数据结果，即在满足本构非退化条件的紧致可见区域中，证明了局部唯一性和Lipschitz稳定性。

Conclusion: 通过引入本构关系耦合，可以从单一边界测量同时恢复波动方程的初始源和声速，并在适当几何条件下达到Lipschitz稳定性，克服了线性化问题固有的不稳定性。

Abstract: We study the simultaneous recovery of the initial source and sound speed for the scalar wave equation from a single boundary measurement. Although the recovery of either parameter separately is well understood under suitable geometric hypotheses, simultaneous recovery remains open in general, and stable recovery is further obstructed by the inherent instability of the linearized problem. We show that both uniqueness and stability can be obtained when the two unknowns are coupled through a prescribed constitutive relation arising from a common underlying material. Under a quantitative nondegeneracy condition, motivated by calibrated material regimes, the coupled inverse problem reduces to a single inverse source problem. Applying the microlocal and Carleman framework of Stefanov and Uhlmann to this reduced problem, we establish global uniqueness and Lipschitz stability under geometric conditions involving strictly convex foliations and geodesic visibility. We also obtain partial-data results, proving local uniqueness and Lipschitz stability in compact visible regions where the constitutive nondegeneracy condition holds.

### [19] [The Liouville equation on Riemannian surfaces: the role of volume growth in classification and rigidity results](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19838)
*Giulio Ciraolo,Alberto Farina,Michele Gatti*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究非负Ricci曲率的完备非紧Riemann曲面上的Liouville方程 -Δu = e^u，在仅假设解具有某种渐近下界条件下，建立了解与流形本身的分类定理，揭示了流形体积增长与解的分类之间的密切联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非负Ricci曲率的完备非紧Riemann曲面上，Liouville方程解的完全分类问题尚未解决。已有分类结果通常需要较强的全局条件（如有限总质量或解的整体有界性），本文旨在仅利用解的渐近下界这一较弱条件，建立更一般的分类理论，并探讨其结果的最优性。

Method: 利用非负Ricci曲率流形的几何分析工具（如体积增长估计、极坐标下的Laplacian比较定理等），结合Liouville方程的PDE分析方法（如移动平面法、爆破分析、梯度估计等），将几何量（体积增长）与分析量（解的渐近行为）建立定量联系，进而分类。

Result: 建立了流形体积增长与Liouville方程解的分类之间的对应关系：对于不同体积增长速率的流形，解呈现出不同的结构特征（如径向对称解、对数型解等）。同时给出了流形自身的分类（如欧氏平面、抛物型流形等）。

Conclusion: 非负Ricci曲率完备非紧Riemann曲面上Liouville方程的解的分类与流形的体积增长密切相关，这一关系是双向的：体积增长限制了解的形式，而解的存在性也约束了流形的几何结构。所得分类结果在某种意义下是最优的。

Abstract: We study the Liouville equation $-Δu = e^u$ on a complete, connected, non-compact, boundaryless Riemannian surface $(M, g)$ with non-negative Ricci curvature. Assuming only some asymptotic lower bound on the solution, we establish classification results for both the solutions and the ambient manifold, discussing also their optimality. Our results reveal a close connection between the volume growth of the manifold and the classification of both the solutions and the underlying manifold.

</details>


### [20] [Nonlinear Instability in the 2D Kuramoto-Sivashinsky equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19887)
*David M. Ambrose,Anna L. Mazzucato,Riccardo Montalto*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了二维方形环面上Kuramoto-Sivashinsky方程（KSE）的非线性不稳定性。针对尺寸足够大的环面（L > π），线性化算子存在有限个增长模。主要结果表明：存在一个有限维初始数据流形，其规模可任意小，但对应解会在对数时间内增长到O(1)量级。证明结合了近似解构造、带指数权的固定点论证以及基于精细能量估计和仿微分算子的延拓论证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维KSE的长时行为分析在很大程度上仍是开放问题，现有全局存在性结果仅适用于足够小的环面或各向异性薄区域，主要原因在于缺乏良好的先验估计。本文旨在从非线性层面分析增长模周围的不稳定性，以推动对该方程长时间行为的理解。

Method: 1) 对最大增长模λ₀进行尖锐的定量近似解构造，该解从线性最大增长模分岔而来；2) 采用带指数权的固定点论证构造局部时间解；3) 基于精细能量估计和仿微分（para-differential）演算的延拓论证，将解延拓到更长的时间尺度。

Result: 证明了对任意小的ε>0，存在一个有限维初始数据流形，其大小为ε，对应的解在O(log(ε⁻¹))时间尺度内增长到O(1)量级，即从任意小的扰动出发，系统会产生显著的非线性不稳定性。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了二维KSE在较大环面上从线性增长模出发的非线性失稳机制，为理解该方程在二维情形下的长时间行为提供了重要理论依据和新的分析框架。

Abstract: In this paper we analyze the Kuramoto-Sivashinsky equation (KSE), a model of flame-front propagation, on a two-dimensional square torus of arbitrary size $2 L$ with $L > π$. In this case, the linearized equation at the origin admits a finite number of growing modes, which corresponds to the positive eigenvalues of the linear operator $- Δ^2 - Δ$. The problem of analyzing the long-time behavior of solutions of the 2D KSE in two spatial dimensions remains largely open; the only global existence results are for sufficiently small tori, or for sufficiently anisotropic and thin domains, due to the lack of good a priori estimates.
  The main purpose of this paper is to analyze the instability around growing modes at the nonlinear level. More precisely, we consider the maximal growing mode $λ_0$ and we show that there is a finite dimensional manifold of initial data of size $\varepsilon$ arbitrarily small such that the corresponding solutions become of size $O(1)$ over a time-scale of order ${\rm log}(\varepsilon^{- 1})$. The proof is based on several ingredients such as a sharp quantitative construction of an approximate solution bifurcating from the maximal linearly growing mode, a fixed point argument with exponential weights to construct local in time solutions, and a continuation argument based on sharp energy estimates and para-differential calculus.

### [24] [Equilibria and linear stability for the Boltzmann equation with radial anharmonic confining potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20025)
*Ling-bing He,Jie Ji,Wu-wei Li*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 该论文研究了全空间径向非调和约束势（p>2 和 1<p<2）下的玻尔兹曼方程，分类了所有正质量-能量、熵不变的解（平衡态），分析了线性化算子的五维驻波空间，并证明了半群解在指数加权L²空间中的代数收敛速率，揭示了角动量对非线性渐近吸引的阻碍作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非调和约束势（如|x|^p/p, p>2 或 <x>^p/p, 1<p<2）下，玻尔兹曼方程的平衡态结构和长时间行为尚不清晰。p>2时旋转平衡态的存在性与角动量角色、1<p<2时积分性排除旋转平衡态、以及非线性平衡流形与线性驻波空间的维度不匹配导致的渐近吸引障碍，是主要研究动机。

Method: 首先通过零熵产生条件分类非线性平衡流形；然后对任意平衡态线性化，识别五维驻波空间并用守恒矩构造显式投影；利用远场权转移估计补偿碰撞算子在空间无穷远处的退化性；最后在指数加权L²空间中分析半群解的收敛性。

Result: p>2时，非线性平衡流形由质量、温度和角动量三分量参数化（五维）；1<p<2时仅由质量和能量参数化（二维）。碰撞算子可归一化为C_M e^{-φ(x)} L，其微观强制系数在空间无穷远处退化，远场权转移估计弥补了该退化。减去驻波投影后，半群解在指数加权L²空间中代数收敛，速率由增长指数p和两权重的间隙控制（损失任意小）。对于1<p<2，二维非线性平衡流形与五维线性驻波空间的维度不匹配，导致携带非零角动量的扰动存在非线性渐近吸引的条件性障碍。

Conclusion: 该工作完整刻画了径向非调和约束势下玻尔兹曼方程的平衡态分类与线性化结构，建立了加权空间中的代数收敛理论，并揭示了低增长指数（1<p<2）下角动量守恒对非线性动力学的根本性影响——旋转扰动无法被非线性吸引到静态平衡态。这为理解非调和约束下动力学方程的长时间行为提供了重要理论基础。

Abstract: We study the Boltzmann equation in the whole space under the radial anharmonic confining potentials $Φ(x)=|x|^p/p$ for $p>2$ and $Φ(x)=\langle x\rangle^p/p$ for $1<p<2$. We first classify all positive finite-mass-and-energy entropy-invariant, equivalently zero-entropy-production, solutions. For $p>2$, the nonlinear equilibrium manifold is parametrized by mass, temperature, and the three components of angular momentum; for $1<p<2$, integrability excludes rotating equilibria and only mass and energy remain as equilibrium parameters. We then identify the five-dimensional stationary space of the equation linearized about an arbitrary equilibrium and construct an explicit projection determined by the conserved moments. After normalization, the collision term takes the form $C_Me^{-\widetildeΦ(x)}\mathsf L$, so its microscopic coercivity degenerates at spatial infinity. A far-field weight-transfer estimate compensates for this degeneracy. After subtracting the stationary projection, the corresponding semigroup solution converges algebraically in exponentially weighted $L^2$ spaces. The rate is governed by the growth exponent $p$ and the gap between the two weights, up to an arbitrarily small loss. For $1<p<2$, the mismatch between the two-dimensional nonlinear equilibrium manifold and the five-dimensional linear stationary space yields a conditional obstruction to nonlinear asymptotic attraction for perturbations carrying nonzero angular momentum.

### [25] [Kinetic Fokker-Planck equations with Maxwell boundary conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20076)
*Kyeongbae Kim,Marvin Weidner*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文建立了线性动力学Fokker-Planck方程在Maxwell边界条件下解的正则性理论，将现有文献中仅覆盖极端情况（α=0和α=1）的结果推广到整个中间区间α∈(0,1)。研究表明：系数一致椭圆时解具有Hölder连续性；系数足够光滑时，可达最优边界正则性阶数3/π·arccos(α/2)-1。此外，该方法可推广至包括超弹性碰撞在内的广泛反射边界条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有动力学Fokker-Planck方程的边界正则性理论仅覆盖Maxwell边界条件的两个极端情形（完全漫反射α=0和完全镜面反射α=1），中间过渡区间α∈(0,1)的正则性理论缺失。本文旨在填补这一空白，并发展统一方法以推广至更广泛的反射边界条件。

Method: 采用统一分析框架，通过构造适当的边界层和精细的先验估计，利用拟微分算子和能量方法，结合Hölder空间和Sobolev空间的嵌入定理，推导出不同α取值下解的最优正则性阶数。

Result: 1) 系数一致椭圆时，Maxwell边界条件下解具有Hölder连续性；2) 系数足够光滑时，边界正则性阶数达到3/π·arccos(α/2)-1，且该指数最优；3) 该统一方法可推广至超弹性碰撞等更一般的反射边界条件。

Conclusion: 完整解决了Maxwell边界条件中间区间α∈(0,1)的正则性理论，获得了最优边界正则性指数，并建立了适用于广泛反射边界条件的统一分析框架，为动力学方程边界层理论提供了重要拓展。

Abstract: We develop the boundary regularity theory for solutions to linear kinetic Fokker-Planck equations with Maxwell boundary conditions. These conditions interpolate between diffuse and specular reflection via an accommodation coefficient $α\in [0,1]$. While existing literature is restricted to the extreme cases $α= 0$ and $α= 1$, we resolve the entire intermediate regime $α\in (0,1)$. Specifically, we show that solutions are Hölder continuous if the coefficients are merely uniformly elliptic. Furthermore, for sufficiently smooth coefficients, we establish boundary regularity of order $\frac{3}π \arccos(\fracα{2}) - 1$ up to the grazing set. This exponent is optimal. Beyond Maxwell conditions, we develop a unified approach that extends to a broad class of reflection boundary conditions, including super-elastic collisions.

Abstract: This article concerns sonic-supersonic jet flows issuing from a two-dimensional straight nozzle described by the steady compressible Euler system under the van der Waals equation of state. The flow state is prescribed at the nozzle exit, while the surrounding medium is assumed to be either a vacuum or a static atmosphere with lower pressure. When the flow reaches the sonic state at the nozzle exit, the governing equations become degenerate hyperbolic and the resulting jet flow problem can be formulated as a degenerate free boundary problem. The analysis is further complicated by singular behavior near the endpoints of the nozzle exit. By employing characteristic decompositions and suitable a priori estimates, we establish the global existence of locally Lipschitz continuous sonic-supersonic jet flows expanding into a vacuum. Moreover, in the presence of a static atmosphere with pressure lower than that at the nozzle exit, we prove the local existence of sonic-supersonic jet flows near the nozzle exit.

</details>

Abstract: This paper investigates the principal spectral theory of a nonlocal dispersal operator with coupled diffusion and aims to establish a variational characterization of the spectral bound for the case where the system is not strongly coupled. To overcome this, we reorder the components of the operator using a permutation matrix, thereby decomposing it into suitable suboperators, and characterize the spectral bound of the original operator in terms of the spectral bounds of these suboperators. Building on this principal spectral theory, we provide a variational characterization of the basic reproduction ratio for nonlocal dispersal systems and analyze the dynamical behavior of a class of multi-genotype stem cell regeneration models with epigenetic transitions, both in the presence and absence of gene mutations, without assuming the existence of a principal eigenvalue. Furthermore, we investigate the threshold dynamics when the system is not strongly coupled.

Abstract: For a domain $Ω$ that is a deformation of a unit ball in $\mathbb{R}^n$, we establish the existence of a sequence of local minimizers for the vector Allen-Cahn energy having $n+1$ wells. ### [32] [Native Multi-Dimensional Subquadratic Operators via Input Dependent Long Convolutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19378)
*David R. Wessels,Farhad Ramezanghorbani,David W. Romero,Alireza Moradzadeh,Olivia Viessmann,Maksim Zhdanov,John St. John,Ken Janik,David M Knigge,Yucheng Tang,Erik J Bekkers,Saee Gopal Paliwal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: HyenaND是一种亚二次、全局、输入相关的算子，通过隐式参数化的全局多维卷积核直接作用于多维数据的原生几何结构，在基因组学、计算机视觉、医学成像和PDE建模等任务中，纯HyenaND堆栈匹配强注意力基线精度，混合配置（HyenaND+注意力）则优于纯注意力和基于递归的混合模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有亚二次注意力替代方案在处理多维数据时需要妥协：标准卷积缺乏全局感受野和输入依赖性，而递归模型需要将图像、体积和PDE等数据栅格化为违反空间结构的临时一维扫描顺序。

Method: 提出HyenaND算子，通过隐式参数化的全局、输入相关的多维卷积核直接对多维数据的原生几何结构进行卷积操作；CUDA实现nSubQ融合了FFT-卷积路径，将HyenaND的O(L log L)缩放转化为实际墙钟加速。

Result: 在长上下文基因组学、计算机视觉、医学成像和PDE建模任务中，纯HyenaND堆栈匹配强注意力基线的精度；混合配置（HyenaND与注意力层交错）在性能上优于纯注意力和基于递归的强混合模型。

Conclusion: HyenaND作为亚二次算子能有效处理多维数据，且与注意力机制互补，混合模型能取得更优性能。

Abstract: Subquadratic alternatives to attention require compromises when applied to multi-dimensional data: standard convolutions lack global receptive fields and input dependency, while recurrent models require rasterizing data such as images, volumes, and partial differential equation (PDE) into an ad-hoc $1\rm D$ scan order that violates their spatial structure. We introduce \textit{HyenaND}, a subquadratic, global, input-dependent operator that acts directly on the native geometry of multidimensional data through convolutions with implicitly parametrized global, input-dependent multi-dimensional convolutional kernels. Our CUDA implementation, \texttt{nSubQ}, fuses the FFT-convolution path to turn HyenaND's $\mathcal{O}(L \log L)$ scaling into wall-clock speedups. Across long-context genomics, computer vision, medical imaging, and PDE modeling, pure HyenaND stacks match the accuracy of strong attention baselines, while hybrid configurations that interleave HyenaND and attention layers outperform both pure attention and strong recurrence-based hybrids.

### [33] [Bayesian Wind Tunnels for Model Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19379)
*Siddhartha R Dalal,Vishal Misra,Abhay Parekh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了Transformer能否进行贝叶斯模型选择（即从数据中识别正确的假设类）。通过设计“贝叶斯风洞”环境，发现2.8M参数Transformer在纯关系型任务（固定点自由对合）上能达到0.01比特的贝叶斯最优熵一致性，并在非嵌套比较（对合vs三循环）中实现模型选择。但在需要算术运算（模加/模乘）时，模型选择在整数tokens上成功，在透明符号上完全失败，且该边界在112倍参数缩放后依然存在。进一步实验表明关键因素是语义稳定性而非整数身份。前沿LLM表现出定性贝叶斯行为但存在约55倍的校准差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前工作已证明Transformer能在固定假设类内进行精确贝叶斯滤波，但能否进行贝叶斯模型选择（即识别正确的假设类）尚不清楚。本文旨在探究Transformer在模型选择任务上的能力及其局限性。

Method: 设计模型选择贝叶斯风洞环境，其中ground-truth后验概率可闭式计算。使用固定点自由对合（f(f(x))=x）作为纯关系型任务，以及模加/模乘作为算术型任务。通过整数tokens与透明符号（每episode含义变化）对比，控制参数规模（2.8M至316M），并设计稳定性控制实验和头部子任务诊断。

Result: 1) 纯关系型任务：2.8M参数Transformer在固定点自由对合上达到0.01比特熵一致性，非嵌套比较（对合vs三循环）中类后验MAE低于0.001。2) 算术型任务：整数tokens成功，透明符号完全失败，该边界在112倍参数缩放后仍然存在。3) 稳定性控制：固定重标定的透明符号成功（0.009-bit MAE）。4) 头部诊断：失败源于头部反转与算术的组合而非头部解析本身。5) 前沿LLM：定性贝叶斯行为但校准差距约55倍。

Conclusion: Transformer能够进行真正的贝叶斯模型选择，但存在关键边界条件：当判别性统计量需要算术运算时，模型选择要求输入具有稳定语义（如整数）而非每episode变化的透明符号。这一边界对模型缩放鲁棒，表明其可能源于Transformer架构的固有局限性而非容量不足。

Abstract: Prior work has shown that transformers can perform exact Bayesian filtering within a fixed
  hypothesis class. Can they also perform Bayesian model selection -- identifying the correct
  hypothesis class from data? We introduce model-selection Bayesian wind tunnels: controlled
  environments where ground-truth posteriors over hypothesis classes are available in closed
  form. Using fixed-point-free involutions -- whose defining property f(f(x))=x is purely
  relational -- a 2.8M-parameter transformer achieves 0.01-bit entropy agreement with the
  Bayesian optimum (3 seeds), with both integer tokens and opaque symbols whose meanings
  change every episode. This extends to non-nested comparisons: involutions vs. 3-cycles
  (where neither class is a subset of the other) achieve class-posterior MAE under 0.001,
  demonstrating genuine model selection beyond simplicity/subset bias. We then identify a
  sharp perceptual access condition: when the discriminative statistic requires arithmetic --
  modular addition (rotations) or multiplication (f(x)=cx mod p) -- model selection succeeds
  with integer tokens but fails completely with opaque symbols, and this boundary persists
  under 112x scaling (2.8M to 316M parameters). A stationarity control confirms the operative
  factor: opaque tokens with a fixed relabeling succeed (0.009-bit MAE), showing that stable
  semantics, not integer identity, enable circuit compilation. Header subtask diagnostics
  localize the failure to the composition of header inversion with arithmetic rather than
  header parsing itself. Probing frontier LLMs on the same tasks shows qualitative Bayesian
  behavior but a large calibration gap (~55x), measured through lossy probes and therefore
  directional rather than exact.

</details>


### [34] [CruiseBench: A Real-Flight-Aligned N-CMAPSS Benchmark for Engine RUL Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19380)
*Pu Cheng,Qiang Miao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对N-CMAPSS数据集因全飞行记录数据量大、退化与运行状态耦合导致评估控制困难的问题，提出CruiseBench基准——基于巡航阶段数据的RUL预测子基准。通过引入CPM-N-CMAPSS掩码提取巡航区间，采用固定协议（排除虚拟传感器/健康参数/元数据，保留原始分辨率窗口，统一RUL上限），在LSTM、GRU、TCN、TSMixer等模型上建立基线。TSMixer取得最佳性能（RMSE 3.4±1.71），消融实验验证了飞行阶段选择、时间降采样方法和RUL上限阈值的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: N-CMAPSS数据集虽通过真实飞行剖面和全飞行时间序列增强了数据真实性，但全飞行记录导致数据量大、退化信号与运行工况变化相互耦合，削弱了评估控制能力，使得预处理选择复杂化，难以直接比较RUL建模性能。因此需要构建一个可控、可复现的RUL基准。

Method: 提出CPM-N-CMAPSS掩码工具，采用共同高度法识别各子数据集的巡航区间；构建CruiseBench基准，固定输入特征（场景描述符+测量传感器，排除虚拟传感器、健康参数和元数据），保留原生分辨率窗口，应用数据集级RUL上限；在LSTM、GRU、TCN、TSMixer四种模型上进行实验和消融分析。

Result: 在CruiseBench-eta5-W256-S10设置下，TSMixer取得最低平均RMSE（3.4±1.71）和最低Saxena得分（(2.50±2.99)×10⁴）；消融实验表明飞行阶段选择、时间降采样方法和RUL上限阈值显著影响结果。

Conclusion: CruiseBench通过固定巡航阶段协议提供了可复现的RUL模型比较子基准；CPM-N-CMAPSS为后续迁移学习和域自适应研究提供了阶段特定的数据基础。

Abstract: Remaining useful life (RUL) prediction estimates how long an engine can continue safe operation and is central to maintenance planning. N-CMAPSS extends C-MAPSS by simulating run-to-failure aero-engine trajectories using recorded real-flight profiles and retaining complete within-flight time series rather than cycle-level snapshots. However, this added realism reduces evaluation control because full-flight records increase data volume and entangle degradation cues with operating-regime variation, complicating preprocessing choices and direct comparisons of RUL modeling performance. To mitigate this issue, this paper proposes CruiseBench, a cruise-stage RUL benchmark derived from N-CMAPSS. It introduces CPM-N-CMAPSS (Cruising-Period Mask for N-CMAPSS), a mask artifact that stores cycle-local cruising intervals identified by the common-altitude method for the nine accessible subdatasets. CruiseBench applies a fixed protocol to the masked rows, using scenario descriptors and measured sensors as inputs while excluding virtual sensors, health parameters, and auxiliary metadata from the feature tensor, preserving native-resolution windows, and applying dataset-wise RUL caps. Experiments with LSTM, GRU, TCN, and TSMixer provide baseline results for this setting. Under CruiseBench-eta5-W256-S10, TSMixer obtains the lowest average RMSE, $3.4\pm1.71$, and Saxena score, $(2.50\pm2.99)\times 10^{4}$. Ablation studies show that flight-stage selection, temporal downscaling method, and RUL-cap threshold affect reported results. With its fixed cruise-stage protocol, CruiseBench provides a reproducible sub-benchmark for controlled RUL model comparison and CPM-N-CMAPSS provides a stage-specific data foundation for future transfer-learning and domain-adaptation studies.

### [35] [Scale-Aware Learning of Chaotic Dynamics on Unstructured Meshes via Binned Spectral Losses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19387)
*Kanad Sen,Romit Maulik*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出将基于傅里叶频带的谱功率损失函数扩展至非结构化网格，利用图拉普拉斯算子定义频率分解，通过切比雪夫多项式近似和多层级图架构（GLEAM）实现高效计算，从而提升非结构化网格上非线性混沌动力系统代理模型的长时程滚动预测 fidelity 和统计不变性保持能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高维非线性混沌动力系统的代理建模需要在保点精度的同时保留物理场的尺度相关结构。现有基于傅里叶频带的谱损失函数适用于结构化网格，但非结构化网格上缺乏标准傅里叶基，无法直接应用该监督机制。

Method: 1) 将傅里叶频带替换为图拉普拉斯频带，利用图拉普拉斯特征空间实现频带功率匹配的图模拟；2) 采用稀疏切比雪夫多项式图滤波器替代精确频带投影器，避免显式特征分解；3) 提出GLEAM（Graph Laplacian Energy Alignment for Meshes），在多层级图架构中跨图层次施加保留子空间的尺度感知监督，在自回归 rollout 过程中正则化粗细表征。

Result: 所提出的谱损失方法在非结构化网格湍流预测任务中，相比确定性基线方法，显著提升了长时程 rollout fidelity，并更好地保持了统计不变量。

Conclusion: 基于图拉普拉斯的频带谱功率损失及其可扩展近似（切比雪夫滤波器和GLEAM）为非结构化网格上的非线性动力系统代理建模提供了一种有效的尺度感知监督机制，在保持物理结构方面优于传统确定性方法。

Abstract: Surrogate modeling for high-dimensional nonlinear dynamical systems that exhibit chaos requires mechanisms that preserve not only pointwise accuracy but also the scale-dependent structure of physical fields. Bandwise spectral power losses, such as the binned spectral loss function, provide such supervision on structured grids, where Fourier modes define a standard frequency decomposition. On irregular meshes, however, no canonical Fourier basis exists, and spectral representations must be constructed from graph operators induced by mesh connectivity and geometry. In this study, we extend the binned spectral power loss for application to unstructured-mesh surrogate modeling of nonlinear dynamical systems. This is obtained by replacing Fourier bands with graph-Laplacian frequency bands, and we provide scalable Chebyshev and multilevel approximations for improving long-horizon rollout fidelity. In its full-spectrum form, our approach uses graph Laplacian eigenspaces to provide a graph analogue of Fourier band-power matching, but incurs the high cost of spectral decomposition. As a scalable approximation, we replace exact band projectors with sparse Chebyshev polynomial graph filters, avoiding explicit eigendecomposition. When utilizing multilevel graph architectures, we introduce Graph Laplacian Energy Alignment for Meshes (GLEAM), which applies retained-subspace scale-aware supervision across graph hierarchies so that coarse and fine representations are regularized during autoregressive rollout. Our results show that the proposed spectral losses improve long-horizon rollout fidelity and preserve statistical invariants for the forecasting of turbulent flows on unstructured meshes, compared to deterministic baselines.

</details>

### [38] [SUM: Unified Geometric Surgery on Spatio-Temporal Adaptation Vectors for Federated Class Incremental Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19384)
*Jaeik Kim,Jaeyoung Do*

TL;DR: 本文提出SUM框架，通过统一几何手术方法处理联邦类增量学习中的时空灾难性遗忘问题，仅需服务端操作即可实现22%的性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联邦类增量学习（FCIL）中，联邦学习（空间异质性）和持续学习（时间任务序列）的组合产生了时空灾难性遗忘（ST-CF）。现有方法分别处理空间和时间干扰，导致额外的客户端计算或通信开销，且未能规范聚合过程中更新的方向性交互。

Method: 将FCIL重新解释为统一的多任务学习问题，客户端和任务更新均表示为共享参数空间中的适应向量。提出SUM框架，在服务端聚合阶段对适应向量进行几何手术：空间SUM缓解轮内客户端间干扰，因果在线时间SUM消除跨任务干扰，无需额外客户端计算、通信或内存。

Result: 在多种视觉和语言基准上，SUM相比现有FCIL方法提升高达22%，同时对不可靠客户端保持鲁棒性且计算高效。

Conclusion: 通过统一几何视角处理时空干扰的耦合问题，SUM是一种纯服务端的高效FCIL解决方案，有效解决了ST-CF并取得了显著性能提升。

Abstract: Real-world intelligent systems often require both distributed collaboration across data-isolated clients and continual adaptation to evolving tasks. This setting naturally gives rise to Federated Class Incremental Learning (FCIL), which combines Federated Learning (FL) and Continual Learning (CL). However, their combination introduces two coupled sources of interference: spatial interference from heterogeneous clients and temporal interference from sequential tasks, jointly leading to Spatial-Temporal Catastrophic Forgetting (ST-CF). Existing approaches typically address spatial and temporal interference with separate mechanisms, often incurring additional client-side computation or communication, while leaving directional interactions among updates during aggregation unregulated. In this paper, we reinterpret FCIL as a unified multi-task learning problem, where both client and task updates are represented as adaptation vectors in a shared parameter space. Based on this view, we propose Unified Geometric Surgery on Spatio-Temporal Adaptation Vectors (SUM), a purely server-side framework that performs geometric surgery on adaptation vectors during aggregation. Spatial SUM mitigates client-level interference within each round, while causal online temporal SUM removes cross-task interference over time without additional client-side computation, communication, or memory beyond standard federated training. Empirically, SUM achieves up to 22% improvement over prior FCIL methods across diverse vision and language benchmarks while remaining robust to unreliable clients and maintaining computational efficiency.

### [41] [Interval and fuzzy physics-augmented neural networks (iPANN and fPANN) for uncertainty quantification and propagation in constitutive modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20339)

We propose interval and fuzzy physics-augmented neural networks (iPANNs and fPANNs) for uncertainty-aware hyperelastic constitutive modeling. iPANNs learn sparse lower, mean, and upper free energy density branches whose stresses, obtained by automatic differentiation, ultimately enclose noisy stress observations. In contrast to this deterministic interval description, fPANNs embed the learned iPANN branches into a fuzzy-set representation through alpha-cut interpolation, yielding a nested family of admissible responses. iPANNs and fPANNs encode mechanistic constraints - preserving objectivity, consistency and promoting polyconvexity - and smoothed L0 regularization promotes interpretable energy representations. The results show that the learned bounds enclose noisy stress observations while generalizing to the test set. Further, we examine the propagation of uncertainty through the mean, upper and lower bound predictions of the learned iPANN models in a finite element setting. The proposed framework provides a compact, physics-consistent route for distribution-free aleatoric uncertainty quantification in hyperelastic constitutive modeling, and propagation in downstream finite element simulations.

Abstract: Cross-paper comparison of sparse autoencoder (SAE) interpretability often relies on autointerpretability scores. In this evaluation pipeline, a language model (LM) explains each feature, and another LM scores the explanation. For these comparisons to be meaningful, scores must reflect stable properties of the features rather than confounding aspects of the evaluation pipeline. Through systematic experiments across four metrics (simulation, detection, fuzzing, purity), two models (Pythia-160M, Apertus-8B), and four axes of methodological variation, we show that this assumption does not hold. Specifically, we find that R1) methodological variance collectively exceeds architectural variance across all metrics and tested models; R2) each metric exhibits a distinct instability profile, with detection being the most stable and fuzzing unreliable across all conditions; R3) top-k feature rankings do not stay consistent across corpus and draw conditions, masking per-feature instability behind stable mean scores; a failure that cannot be detected by monitoring explanation similarity alone. These findings suggest that cross-paper comparisons based on autointerpretability scores may reflect pipeline differences rather than architectural differences, with implications for the ongoing debate on SAE utility. More broadly, unreliable evaluation slows progress in interpretability research at a time when reliable tools for understanding AI systems are needed. To support evaluation, we contribute a variance decomposition approach, a Stability Check, and a Minimum Reporting Checklist.

Each case is solved to high fidelity with a verified discrete-ordinates solver, and an average relative L_2 error norm is used to characterize the quality of the inferred maps. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究正交化mLSTM记忆矩阵读取操作（5次Newton-Schulz迭代）为何能改善噪声联想召回，并澄清该改进的本质机制——是记忆增强还是学习动态的重新调节。

Method: 通过三种分析建立：（1）自一致性——对比Mesa层（精确递归最小二乘读取）、直通估计、delta规则写入、冻结随机键、普通归一化等方法；（2）均匀性——在学习率×难度的网格上测量逃脱风险；（3）可移除性——在推理时应用于失败模型、在触发逃脱后退火。此外通过解码记忆状态直接观察存储内容，并建模逃脱风险的热/噪声定律。

Result: 正交化读操作将逃脱风险提升约6倍，且与任务难度无关；拓宽了可行学习率走廊；失败模型在记忆状态中存储了约一半的可线性恢复关联，平台期是读取失败而非写入失败；原始vocab-96结果是大批量噪声条件而非容量条件。

Conclusion: 联想召回基准测试中架构性能的提升部分反映的是可训练性而非记忆容量；该实验设置可作为“涌现”现象的完整仪器化模型系统，其中尖锐的行为阈值源于对逐渐积累结构的截断度量。

Abstract: A recent report finds that orthogonalizing the mLSTM memory matrix at read time (five Newton-Schulz iterations, trained through) substantially improves noisy associative recall. The effect replicates, but it is not a memory improvement. Training on this task is a long chance plateau followed by a sharp escape, and the orthogonalized read acts by re-conditioning the learning problem during the plateau. Three properties establish this. It must be self-consistent: an exact recursive least-squares read (the Mesa layer) reproduces it, while straight-through halves, delta-rule writes, frozen random keys, and plain normalization all fail. It is uniform: across a learning-rate x hardness grid it multiplies the escape hazard roughly six-fold with no detectable hardness dependence, widening the workable learning-rate corridor that narrows for the baseline. And it is removable: applied to failed models at inference it rescues none, and annealed away on an escape-triggered schedule it leaves numerically stock mLSTMs at full accuracy. Much of the published gain needs no architecture at all -- solved-rate at a fixed budget measures escape hazard, which follows a heat/noise law (learning-rate elasticity +3.0, gradient-noise elasticity -1.65) under which the original vocab-96 result is a large-batch noise condition rather than a capacity one. Decoding the memory state directly shows failed models carry roughly half their associations in linearly recoverable form: the plateau is a readout failure over half-written storage. Two conclusions travel beyond the intervention: recall benchmarks used for architecture selection partly measure trainability, and the system is a fully instrumented model organism of "emergence," in which a sharp behavioral threshold demonstrably arises from a censored metric over gradually accumulating structure.

</details>


### [45] [LAARA: Layer-Aware Adaptive Rank Allocation for Parameter-Efficient Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19391)
*Ashutosh Tripathi,Surya Deep Singh,Pranab Sahoo,Sriparna Saha*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LAARA是一种基于Fisher信息引导的自适应秩分配框架，通过轻量级对角Fisher估计动态分配各层的LoRA秩，在GLUE和MathInstruct基准上以更少参数匹配或超越LoRA、AdaLoRA、DyLoRA等SOTA方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LoRA方法对所有Transformer层分配相同的适配器秩，忽略了不同层在微调中的异质性需求，理论上和经验上证明均匀秩分配是次优的。

Method: LAARA利用训练过程中计算的轻量级对角Fisher估计进行动态秩分配，结合投影归一化、对数压缩、混合适配器重要性估计以及投票变更阻尼机制，实现稳定高效的秩自适应分配，且无需搜索。

Result: 在GLUE和MathInstruct基准上的实验表明，LAARA在显著减少可训练参数的情况下，性能一致匹配或超越LoRA、AdaLoRA、DyLoRA、Bitfit等现有方法。

Conclusion: Fisher引导的秩分配为参数高效微调提供了一种有原理且有效的自适应基础。

Abstract: Low-Rank Adaptation is widely used for parameter-efficient fine-tuning, yet existing methods typically assign the same adapter rank to every transformer layer despite their heterogeneous adaptation requirements. In this work, we show theoretically and empirically that uniform rank allocation is fundamentally suboptimal. Motivated by this observation, we propose LAARA (Layer Aware Adaptive Rank Allocation framework), a search-free framework that dynamically allocates ranks using lightweight diagonal Fisher estimates computed during training. LAARA combines projection-wise normalization, logarithmic compression, blended adapter importance estimation, and a vote-to-change dampening mechanism to produce stable and efficient rank adaptation. Experiments on GLUE and MathInstruct benchmark demonstrate that LAARA consistently matches or outperforms popular state of the art approaches such as LoRA, AdaLoRA, DyLoRA, and Bitfit while using significantly fewer trainable parameters. Our results show that Fisher-guided rank allocation provides a principled and effective foundation for adaptive parameter-efficient fine-tuning. The code is publicly available at: https://anonymous.4open.science/r/LAARA-D305/LAARA.py

### [46] [Total Variation Distance Estimation in Autoregressive Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19510)
*Eric Price,Kevin Tian,Zhiyang Xun,Yusong Zhu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在大语言模型部署中，由于不同推理引擎（如SGLang和vLLM）使用不同的实现优化，导致“相同模型”产生不同输出分布的问题。作者提出了在三种访问模型下估计两个自回归分布之间总变差距离（TV距离）的算法：样本访问（$\widetilde{O}(n^2 K/\varepsilon^2)$查询）、logits访问（$O(n/\varepsilon^2)$查询，最优）和带噪logits访问（$\widetilde{O}((n+n^2\sigma^2)/\varepsilon^2)$查询）。实验验证了算法的实用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代LLM部署中，即使使用相同权重，不同的推理引擎（如SGLang和vLLM）由于批处理、自定义内核、量化等优化手段的不同，会产生有意义的分布差异。需要估计这些分布之间的总变差距离，以量化这种差异。

Method: 提出了三种访问模型下的TV距离估计算法：(1) 样本访问下使用$\widetilde{O}(n^2 K/\varepsilon^2)$查询；(2) logits访问下使用$O(n/\varepsilon^2)$查询；(3) 带噪logits访问下使用$\widetilde{O}((n+n^2\sigma^2)/\varepsilon^2)$查询。并进行了实验评估。

Result: 样本访问算法改进了Meel等人(2025)的$\widetilde{O}(n^3 m/\varepsilon^5)$查询复杂度至$\widetilde{O}(n^2 K/\varepsilon^2)$；logits访问算法达到最优$O(n/\varepsilon^2)$；带噪logits算法实现了平滑插值。实验表明TV距离在KL散度无穷大时仍可估计。

Conclusion: 提出的TV距离估计算法在理论上具有更优或最优的查询复杂度，在实践中能够有效衡量不同LLM推理引擎之间的分布差异，且比KL散度更具鲁棒性。

Abstract: Modern LLM deployments use a number of implementation choices and inference optimizations (e.g., batching, custom kernels, and quantization) on top of fixed weights, so two engines serving "the same model" can produce meaningfully different distributions. We study the problem of estimating the total variation (TV) distance between two length-$n$ autoregressive distributions to additive error $\varepsilon$, under three access models. (1) Under sample access, we use $\widetilde{O}(n^2 K/\varepsilon^2)$ queries, where $K$ is the maximum support of the next-token distribution. This improves upon the $\widetilde{O}(n^3 m/\varepsilon^5)$-query estimator of Meel et al. (2025), where $m \geq K$ is the total size of the token alphabet. (2) Under logit access, we use $O(n/\varepsilon^2)$ queries, and this is tight. (3) Under noisy logit access, we smoothly interpolate between the above two guarantees: if probability values are given to relative error $σ$, we use $\widetilde{O}((n+n^2σ^2)/\varepsilon^2)$ queries. We complement our theoretical results with an empirical evaluation of our algorithms, for example measuring the distance between SGLang and vLLM serving identical weights. Our experiments highlight the robustness and practicality of estimating the total variation distance, which remains estimable where the KL divergence is infinite. Our code is available at https://github.com/XunZhiyang/llm-tv-estimation.

</details>

Specifically, we use a variety of techniques including kNearest Neighbors (k-NN) and Geographic Information Systems (GIS) to join arsenic measurement points from across the United States by location. Building on this dataset, we evaluate a diverse suite of machine learning models, including tree-based ensemble approaches, multilayer perceptrons, and spatially aware graph neural networks (GNN). Our findings show that while gradient-boosted trees are still considered state-of-the-art in the field of tabular data, GNNs are able to further account for spatial dependence to match or outperform the results of gradient-boosted trees. These results demonstrate that graph-based and spatially informed learning can enhance environmental prediction and provide a foundation for improved groundwater risk mapping and monitoring.

### [48] [Efficient Clustering with Provable Guardrails for LLM Inference at Scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19704)
*Longshaokan Wang,Wai Tsang Keung,Punit Ghodasara,Roman Wang,Ali Dashti,Francesc Moreno-Noguer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种两阶段聚类算法，通过Mini-batch K-Means初始化结合Set Cover启发式选择代表点，在保证每个样本与同类代表点相似度及分类属性匹配的前提下，将LLM推理成本降低50倍，支持3800万用户规模的工业部署。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模LLM应用受限于推理成本和延迟。现有聚类方法无法同时保证(1)样本与代表点之间的最小相似度、(2)分类属性的精确匹配、(3)千万级样本的可扩展性。

Method: 两阶段算法：第一阶段用Mini-batch K-Means生成初始聚类；第二阶段在初始聚类内贪心选择代表点，等价于嵌入空间中α-球的Set Cover的Johnson-Chvatal启发式，严格保证相似度阈值和属性匹配约束。时间复杂度O(nd + n²d/K)，空间复杂度O(nd + n²/K²)，当K与n成比例增长时对n线性。

Result: 与常见聚类方法相比，该方法不仅提供每个样本的质量保障，且运行速度快10-1000倍，能处理大多数标准方法不可行的数据规模。在3800万客户的基于人设的推荐系统中，将下游成本和延迟降低50倍，同时保持个性化效果，并解锁了生产上线。

Conclusion: 该方法在理论上实现了可扩展的带约束聚类，在实践中证明了大规模LLM应用通过输入聚类大幅降低推理成本的同时不牺牲输出质量的可行性。

Abstract: Scaling LLM-based applications to millions of users is bottlenecked by the inference cost and latency of modern foundation models. A natural fix is to cluster the inputs and call the LLM only on cluster representatives, letting other members inherit the output -- but this is only safe if each member is measurably close to its representative. Existing clustering methods do not offer such per-sample quality control at scale: none jointly guarantee a minimal within-cluster similarity, exact matching of categorical attributes, and scalability to tens of millions of samples. We propose a two-stage algorithm that generates initial clusters with Mini-batch K-Means, then greedily selects representatives within each initial cluster -- a step equivalent to the Johnson-Chvatal heuristic for Set Cover over alpha-balls in embedding space. The algorithm enforces the similarity and attribute guardrails exactly by construction, and runs in $O(nd + n^2 d/K)$ time and $O(nd + n^2/K^2)$ memory for $n$ samples, feature dimension $d$, and $K$ initial clusters -- linear in $n$ when $K$ grows proportionally with $n$. We provide benchmarks against common clustering methods on internal and public datasets: our method not only delivers per-sample guardrails but also runs 10-1000x faster and scales to data sizes where most standard methods become intractable. Deployed on 38 million customers for a persona-based recommender, the clustering method cut downstream cost and latency by 50-fold while preserving personalization and unblocked the production launch.

### [49] [Decodable but Not Detectable: A Leakage Fingerprint for Near-OOD Benchmarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19393)
*Vishnu Bindu Balachandran*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文发现并纠正了OOD检测基准中的数据泄露问题：由于训练集包含被误标为OOD的类别，导致评测指标异常（AUROC低于随机水平0.5）。通过删除泄露类别重新训练，得分从0.326提升至0.911。作者提出了泄露指纹（有监督可解码性接近完美+无监督检测崩溃低于0.65），并通过52个受控实验和24个自然基准对验证了诊断方法的有效性。最终结论是：扰动信号在监督下可解码但不可检测，且扰动方法并未优于普通马氏距离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在评测基于扰动的OOD检测器时发现异常低的AUROC（0.326），远低于随机水平0.5，经排查发现是由于基准数据泄露——被标记为"OOD"的类别实际上在训练集中出现过，导致检测器正确将其判定为"熟悉"时反而被扣分。

Method: 1) 识别并删除泄露类别，重新训练35个跨领域模型；2) 提出泄露指纹诊断方法：监督可解码性AUROC≈1 + 无监督检测AUROC<0.65；3) 在52组受控设置（20泄露/32干净）和24个自然基准对上验证；4) 分析扰动信号的可解码性与可检测性。

Result: 1) 删除泄露类别后AUROC从0.326提升至0.911；2) 泄露指纹诊断在嵌入空间的灵敏度18/20，特异性31/32；3) 匹配的fit-set排除控制完美20/20；4) 24个自然基准对中仅触发一个（CIFAR-100 vs CIFAR-10）；5) 监督解码AUROC 0.87-1.00，无监督检测全部失败；6) 扰动方法未优于普通马氏距离。

Conclusion: 本文提供了OOD检测基准泄露的修正协议和有效的泄露诊断方法，而非提出新的OOD方法。核心发现是扰动信号在监督下可解码但在无监督下不可检测，且扰动方法本身并不优于基线方法。作者还撤回了先前的一项循环相关性结论。

Abstract: While auditing a perturbation-based OOD detector on a document benchmark, we recorded an AUROC of 0.326 -- well below the 0.5 chance level. The cause is a benchmark leak: the designated "OOD" class is one the model was trained on, so its examples sit inside the in-distribution fit set and the detector is penalized for correctly ranking them as familiar. Deleting the class and retraining 35 models across two domains raises the score to 0.911. We distill the contamination into a leak fingerprint -- near-perfect supervised decodability (AUROC approximately 1) coupled with unsupervised detection collapsed below 0.65 -- and validate it on a controlled battery of 52 settings (20 leaked, 32 clean) across ResNet-50 and ViT-B/16 on CIFAR-10/100, achieving sensitivity 18/20 and specificity 31/32 in embedding space; the matched fit-set-exclusion controls are perfect at 20/20. An in-the-wild audit of 24 standard near/far OOD benchmark pairs fires on exactly one (the intrinsically hard CIFAR-100 vs CIFAR-10 pair) and on no far-OOD pair, confirming specificity and that standard cross-dataset construction is clean. Under the corrected protocol, perturbation signals are decodable but not detectable: a supervised reader recovers the OOD signal (AUROC 0.87-1.00) while no unsupervised detector does, and the perturbation method does not improve on plain Mahalanobis distance. We provide a theoretical account of why and, for transparency, retract an earlier circular correlation. The contributions are a corrected protocol and a validated leak diagnostic, not a new OOD method.

### [50] [Asymptotically Optimal Regret for Reinforcement Learning without Horizon Dependence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19854)
*Runlong Zhou,Zihan Zhang,Maryam Fazel,Simon S. Du*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对有限水平时间齐次表格型MDP，提出了一种新的无遗憾算法，实现了渐近最优的$\tilde O(\sqrt{SAK}+S^8A^3)$遗憾上界，完全消除了对$H$和$\log H$的依赖，匹配了上下文赌博机的下界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前的工作（Zhang et al., 2021）虽然实现了接近最优的遗憾，但仍存在$\log H$因子；后续工作（Zhang et al., 2022）虽然实现了无$H$依赖的遗憾，但多项式因子较大（$S^9A^3$）。本文旨在彻底消除$H$的依赖，同时获得渐近最优的遗憾界。

Method: (1) 利用最优价值函数$V_h^*$关于$h$的单调性；(2) 将价值函数非平凡地投影到$S$维网格上，避免直接联合界导致的$\min\{\log H,S\}$因子；(3) 引入水平截断参数实现基于奖励的探索；(4) 设计保持乐观性和单调性的切割奖励函数；(5) 证明对时间齐次MDP的总偏差新界，控制切割奖励中的裁剪方差项。

Result: 得到了$\tilde O(\sqrt{SAK}+S^8A^3)$的遗憾上界，无$H$依赖，渐近匹配$\Omega(\sqrt{SAK})$下界，显著改进了Zhang et al. (2022)的$\tilde O(\sqrt{S^9A^3K})$。

Conclusion: 本文提出的算法在有限水平时间齐次MDP中实现了无$H$依赖的渐近最优遗憾，消除了$\log H$因子，并通过三项关键技术贡献证明了该界。

Abstract: We study horizon-free regret minimization for finite-horizon time-homogeneous tabular Markov decision processes with $S$ states, $A$ actions, horizon $H$, and per-trajectory total reward bounded by $1$.
  We propose a new algorithm and prove a regret upper bound \[\tilde O(\sqrt{SAK}+S^8A^3)\] with failure probability $δ$, where $K$ is the number of episodes and $\tilde O(\cdot)$ hides $\mathsf{poly}\log(S,A,K,1/δ)$.
  Thus, the regret is $H$-free and asymptotically optimal, matching the contextual-bandit lower bound $Ω(\sqrt{SAK})$ up to logarithmic factors. This completely removes the $\log H$ dependence from the previous $\tilde O(\sqrt{SAK\log H}+S^2A\log H)$ guarantee of Zhang et al. (2021), and drastically improves the prior best horizon-free regret $\tilde O(\sqrt{S^9A^3K})$ of Zhang et al. (2022) asymptotically.
  The main technical difficulty is that the optimal value functions $\{V_h^*\}_{h=1}^H$ are time-inhomogeneous even though the transition kernel is time-homogeneous. A direct union bound over all value functions typically incurs an additional $\min\{\log H,S\}$ factor. We avoid this factor by (i) exploiting the monotonicity of $V_h^*$ in $h$ and (ii) non-trivially projecting the value functions onto an $S$-dimensional grid.
  Our analysis relies on three additional ingredients. First, we introduce a horizon-truncation argument that enables reward-based exploration and removes the cost of a separate reward-free exploration phase. Second, we design a cutting bonus that preserves both optimism and the monotonicity needed for planning. Third, we prove a new bound on total deviation for time-homogeneous MDPs, which controls the clipped variance terms in the cutting bonus with adjustable polynomial dependence on $S$ and without any dependence on $H$. Together, these tools yield an asymptotically optimal horizon-free regret guarantee.

</details>


### [51] [Cross-Subject Semantic Decoding with Shared-Space Alignment for Generalized Neural Representation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19394)
*Ji-Hoon Heo,Aleksandra Joanna Wisniewska,Seo-Hyun Lee,Seong-Whan Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出跨被试语义解码框架，通过共享响应模型将多被试神经信号对齐到共享潜在空间，再解码为语义嵌入，实现无需重新训练的跨被试泛化，在ECoG语言理解数据上优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 侵入式神经记录中，电极配置、解剖结构和神经信号模式在不同个体间存在显著差异，导致跨被试泛化困难。当前方法通常需要为每个新被试重新训练模型，缺乏通用性。

Method: 基于ECoG自然语言理解数据，利用共享响应模型（Shared Response Model）估计多被试神经响应的共享潜在空间；训练解码器将投影后的神经表征映射为上下文语义嵌入（contextual embeddings）；对留出被试，直接估计其到预定义共享空间的投影，无需重新训练即可应用预训练解码器。

Result: 该框架在各种评估设置下一致优于基线方法，从源被试到留出被试测试的性能下降更小，表明跨被试泛化能力显著提升。

Conclusion: 将神经活动对齐到共享潜在空间并在语义嵌入空间中解码，是提升跨被试泛化的有效策略，能够减少被试特异性差异的同时有效捕获共享的刺激相关表征。

Abstract: Generalizing across subjects remains challenging in invasive neural recordings because electrode configurations, anatomical structures, and neural signal patterns vary substantially across individuals. To investigate such inter-subject variability, we propose a cross-subject semantic decoding framework that aligns neural responses to speech perception from multiple subjects into a shared latent space and learns a mapping from the aligned neural representations to contextual embeddings. More specifically, using electrocorticography data collected during natural language comprehension, we estimate the shared space using the shared response model and train a decoder to predict contextual semantic embeddings from projected neural responses. For a held-out subject, we estimate a subject-specific projection into the predefined shared space, and directly apply the pretrained decoder without any retraining. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed framework consistently outperforms baseline methods across evaluation settings and exhibits a reduced performance drop from source subject to held-out subject testing, indicating improved cross-subject generalization. These results suggest that aligning neural activity into a shared latent space, while decoding in a semantic embedding space, provides an effective strategy for improving cross-subject generalization by reducing subject-specific differences in neural responses while effectively capturing shared stimulus-related representations.

### [52] [Active Inference as a Convex Markov Decision Process](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20152)
*Nikola Milosevic,Nicolás Hinrichs,Nico Scherf*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文证明主动推理（AIF）中的期望自由能（EFE）最小化可被形式化为凸马尔可夫决策过程（MDP），其中认知项引入非线性成分，并通过镜像下降算法与actor-critic方法兼容，最终将主动推理定位为执行性强化学习。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将主动推理（AIF）纳入现代强化学习和优化理论框架，建立EFE最小化与标准强化学习之间的形式化联系，从而为主动推理提供收敛性分析和策略改进保证等理论基础。

Method: 1) 将AIF形式化为策略优化问题，展示闭环控制策略下EFE最小化可表述为凸MDP；2) 分析有限时域、折扣和平均奖励三种EFE形式；3) 推导镜像下降算法，通过对当前状态边缘分布进行局部线性化，得到策略依赖奖励，与actor-critic方法和动态规划兼容。

Result: 1) 实用项在线性预测状态边缘下等价于潜在MDP中的奖励最大化；2) 认知价值引入非线性成分，将主动推理与标准强化学习区分开；3) 认知驱动力被揭示为策略依赖的（执行性）奖励；4) 世界模型学习与策略优化的耦合赋予主动推理执行性强化学习的结构。

Conclusion: 主动推理可被纳入现代强化学习和优化理论框架，获得收敛性分析和原则性策略改进保证，为两个领域的交叉提供理论桥梁。

Abstract: Active Inference (AIF) frames adaptive behavior as the minimization of expected free energy (EFE), combining epistemic and pragmatic objectives within a single variational principle. We frame AIF as policy optimization and show that, for closed-loop control policies, EFE minimization can be formulated as a convex Markov decision process (MDP). In this formulation, the pragmatic terms are linear in the predictive state marginals and therefore equivalent to reward maximization in a latent MDP, while the epistemic value introduces a nonlinear component that distinguishes EFE minimization from standard reinforcement learning. This perspective further reveals the epistemic drive of active inference as a policy-dependent (performative) reward. We analyze finite-horizon, discounted, and average-reward formulations of EFE and derive a mirror descent (MD) algorithm that locally linearizes the objective around the current state marginals, yielding a policy-dependent reward that is compatible with actor-critic methods and dynamic programming. Finally, we argue that coupling world-model learning with policy optimization gives active inference the structure of performative reinforcement learning, providing a route toward grounding active inference within modern reinforcement learning and optimization theory, including convergence analysis and principled policy improvement guarantees.
