Abstract: Conditional optimization tailors decisions to contextual or event information, but its practical use is often limited by the difficulty of learning the relevant conditional distribution from finite samples of a target joint distribution. This challenge is especially acute when target joint data are scarce or unavailable, or when few observations fall in the conditioning region of interest. Related joint data may be available from multiple sources, such as different stores, markets, populations, or operating environments, but these sources may be biased relative to the target distribution and cannot be pooled naively. We develop a distributionally robust framework based on optimal transport (OT) for harnessing such heterogeneous data in conditional optimization. The framework constructs ambiguity sets over joint distributions using OT distances to empirical source distributions and optimizes worst-case conditional performance over plausible target laws. We propose three OT ambiguity sets that capture different ways of using heterogeneous sources: enforcing simultaneous source consistency, aggregating source discrepancies through weights, and centering the ambiguity set at an OT barycenter. We derive tractable reformulations, establish feasibility conditions, discuss parameter choices, and characterize the relationships among the formulations, revealing trade-offs between robustness, information aggregation, and computational complexity. We demonstrate the value of the framework through a conditional assortment problem using demand and product-feature data from multiple stores.

Abstract: We develop a non-parametric approach to refine forecast-error histories for safety stock estimation without relying on error magnitude or recency alone. Using forecast-error data from a fast-moving consumer goods environment, we show that one year of errors is insufficient to characterize service-level risk, while pooling several years is problematic because error distributions change over time. Non-parametric annual comparisons indicate a progressive reduction in bias and dispersion, consistent with learning in the forecasting process. We propose LOWDII (Leave-One-Out Wasserstein Distributional Influence Index), a diagnostic that evaluates the distributional influence of each historical forecast error on the empirical uncertainty distribution used for safety stock calibration. LOWDII identifies observations whose influence is disproportionate to their representativeness, separating transient distortions from persistent tail behaviour without imposing parametric assumptions. We evaluate the method in a discrete-event simulation using subsequent-year demand realizations as validation. The results show that LOWDII achieves the target service level while reducing average stock by 5.1% to 22.6% relative to benchmark methods. From a managerial perspective, LOWDII helps firms translate improvements in the forecasting process into safety stock decisions, avoiding the projection of obsolete historical errors into the future and capturing the economic benefit of lower uncertainty requirements earlier.

### [162] [Continuous-Time Reinforcement Learning for $N$-Player Stochastic Differential Games with Exploratory Policies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19928)
*Jisheng Liu,Jing Zhang*

TL;DR: 本文研究了N人非合作随机微分博弈中的连续时间强化学习。每个玩家采用熵正则化探索策略，最优响应为吉布斯分布，纳什均衡等价于这些条件分布的兼容性。证明了同时最大化Hamiltonian等价于兼容性，并给出了可计算的最优q函数交叉偏导条件。当兼容性失败时，通过坐标路径积分构造可得到近似相关均衡，具有显式KL散度界。该框架扩展至遍历（无限时域）场景，具有局部均匀的O_R(1/γ)渐近速率。

Result: 1) 纳什均衡等价于条件分布的兼容性，且与同时Hamiltonian最大化等价；2) 给出了兼容性的可计算交叉偏导充要条件；3) 解耦和对称博弈下纳什均衡无条件存在；4) 不兼容时构造的近似相关均衡有显式KL散度界，且随γ→∞局部均匀消失；5) 在遍历场景下保持同样的O_R(1/γ)渐近速率。

Conclusion: 建立了多智能体连续时间随机微分博弈的熵正则化强化学习理论框架，完整刻画了纳什均衡的存在条件，并提供了兼容性失败时的近似均衡方案与收敛保证，为多智能体强化学习提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We study continuous-time reinforcement learning for $N$-player noncooperative stochastic differential games. Each player adopts an entropy-regularized exploratory policy; given the others' actions, the optimal response is a Gibbs distribution, and a Nash equilibrium requires these $N$ conditional distributions to be jointly compatible. We prove that the natural equilibrium concept -- simultaneous Hamiltonian maximization -- is equivalent to this compatibility, and establish a necessary and sufficient condition expressed as a computable cross-partial criterion on the optimal $q$-functions. Nash equilibria exist unconditionally for decoupled and symmetric games. When compatibility fails, a coordinate path integral construction yields an approximate correlated equilibrium with explicit quadratic KL-divergence bounds that vanish locally uniformly as the exploration weight $γ\to\infty$. A $q$-function framework for the $N$-player game extends the single-agent $q$-learning theory of [21], with weak martingale characterizations motivating model-free on-policy and off-policy algorithms. The framework extends to the ergodic (infinite-horizon) setting with the same locally uniform $O_R(1/γ)$ asymptotic rates.

*Gabrielė Kasparavičiūtė,Pasquale Grippa,Kjetil Skaugset,Asgeir J. Sørensen,Martin Ludvigsen*

TL;DR: 提出了一种两阶段混合整数线性规划框架，用于海底管道事故响应规划，联合优化海底对接板（SDP）布局和自主水下机器人（AUV）分配，在空间不确定性下最小化最大响应时间和平均响应时间。以挪威Johan Sverdrup油气田为案例（9个SDP选项、33条管道）验证，少量合理布置的SDP即可达到最优性能，并通过成本-时间帕累托分析揭示了部署成本与响应效率的权衡关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决海底管道泄漏事故响应中，在空间不确定性条件下如何联合优化SDP布置和AUV分配，以同时优化最坏情况响应时间和平均响应时间的决策问题。

Method: 两阶段混合整数线性规划（MILP）框架：第一阶段最小化所有潜在泄漏点的最大响应时间；第二阶段在最大响应时间约束下最小化平均响应时间。通过挪威Johan Sverdrup油气田案例进行验证，并进行成本-时间帕累托分析。

Result: 仅需少量合理布置的SDP即可达到最优性能表现；成本与时间之间存在明确的帕累托权衡关系。

Conclusion: 该框架能够为设计具有韧性和成本效益的海底巡检网络提供可操作的指导建议。

Abstract: A two-stage mixed-integer linear programming framework is introduced for subsea pipeline incident response planning, jointly optimizing Subsea Docking Plate (SDP) placement and resident autonomous underwater vehicle allocation to minimize both maximum and average response times under spatial uncertainty. Phase 1 minimizes the maximum response time across all potential leak locations. Phase 2 reduces the average response time subject to the maximum bound. A case study based on the Johan Sverdrup oil and gas field in Norway, with 9 SDP options and 33 pipelines, shows that just a few well-placed SDPs are enough to achieve top performance. A cost versus time Pareto analysis reveals the trade-off between deployment expenditure and response efficiency, providing actionable guidance for designing resilient and cost-effective subsea inspection networks.

</details>


### [164] [Accelerated Stochastic Zeroth-Order Quasar-Convex Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19965)
*Eméric Gbaguidi,Julien Hermant*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文针对光滑拟凸函数在仅能访问零阶随机噪声函数值情况下的无约束最小化问题，设计了一种零阶连续化算法，实现了与光滑凸优化相当的加速收敛保证，并通过镜像步骤改善了稀疏解情况下的维度依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拟凸函数是凸函数的推广，在实际应用中广泛存在，但标准加速方法依赖一阶信息，在零阶（仅函数值）场景下不可用。现有零阶方法收敛速度不理想，亟需设计适用于零阶场景的加速算法。

Method: 采用连续化（continuized）方法替代传统的子空间搜索加速机制，设计了零阶连续化算法，并结合镜像步骤（mirror step）以改善稀疏解场景下的维度依赖性。

Result: 所提算法在光滑拟凸函数上实现了与光滑凸优化相匹配的加速收敛保证，其中收敛速度取决于拟凸性参数；此外，镜像步骤有效改善了维度依赖性，尤其在存在稀疏解时表现更优。

Conclusion: 零阶连续化方法可以绕过对一阶信息的依赖，为拟凸函数的零阶优化提供加速收敛，且镜像步骤有助于提升稀疏场景下的效率。

Abstract: We consider unconstrained minimization of smooth quasar-convex functions when only noisy function evaluations are accessible through a stochastic zeroth-order oracle. For these non-convex functions, the standard acceleration method relies on subspace-search mechanisms that require first-order information, being therefore unavailable in zeroth-order regimes. In contrast, the alternative and less conventional continuized method enable to avoid such mechanisms. In this work, we design a zeroth-order continuized algorithm, leading to accelerated convergence guarantees that parallel those of smooth convex optimization up to a quasar-convexity parameter. Our method incorporates a mirror step, improving the dimension dependence when there exists sparse solution.

### [165] [Order-2 Tightness of Block-Sparse SOS Relaxations for One-Layer ReLU Network Verification with a Matching Input-Sharing Graph](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20013)
*Godai Azuma,Sunyoung Kim,Makoto Yamashita*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文研究单层ReLU网络的验证问题，将输入共享图限制为匹配结构，证明了在该结构下，若每条边满足正则秩一条件，则阶-2块稀疏SOS松弛是紧的。该结果将无边的紧稀疏松弛结果推广到首个具有非平凡双单元交互的稀疏场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Azuma等人已将单层ReLU网络的验证问题建模为二次约束二次规划，并为无边情形和单单元情形建立了紧的半定松弛。本文旨在将这一紧性结果推广到存在双单元交互的稀疏场景，即输入共享图为匹配的情形。

Method: 通过输入共享图表示未定ReLU在盒状输入集上的共享模式，并将图限制为匹配结构，将全局问题分解为孤立顶点块和单边块。对于正则秩一边块，利用两个约化单单元凸包通过一个公共共享标量耦合来精确描述双单元局部集的凸包；结合Azuma等人的单单元紧性结果、Farkas引理和仿射消元，为每个边块建立局部阶-2证书。

Result: 当输入共享图为匹配且每条边满足正则秩一条件时，阶-2块稀疏SOS松弛是紧的。该结果将无边情形的紧稀疏松弛结果推广到首个具有非平凡双单元交互的稀疏设置。

Conclusion: 本文成功将ReLU网络验证问题的紧半定松弛从无边情形推广到匹配结构的稀疏场景，为更复杂的稀疏结构研究提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Azuma, Kim, and Yamashita formulated the verification problem for one-layer ReLU networks as a quadratically constrained quadratic program and established tight semidefinite relaxations for the edgeless case and for one-unit settings. In this work, we represent the sharing pattern of undecided ReLUs over a box input set through an input-sharing graph and focus on the case where this graph is a matching. We then derive an explicit, checkable sufficient condition for the tightness of the order-$2$ block-sparse SOS relaxation associated with the connected-component decomposition of this graph. Under the matching assumption, the global problem decomposes into isolated-vertex blocks and single-edge blocks. The key difficulty, which is absent from the edgeless case, is establishing tightness for a two-unit edge block. For regular rank-one edges, we show that the convex hull of each two-unit local set can be described exactly by two reduced one-unit hulls coupled through a common shared scalar. Combining the one-unit tightness result of Azuma et al. with Farkas' lemma and affine elimination, we obtain a local order-$2$ certificate for each edge block. Isolated-vertex blocks reduce to one-unit problems over box input sets and are therefore handled at the same order. We prove that, when the input-sharing graph is a matching and every edge satisfies the regular rank-one condition, the order-$2$ block-sparse SOS relaxation is tight. This extends the tight sparse relaxation result for the edgeless case to the first sparse setting with a nontrivial two-unit interaction.

</details>


### [166] [Forward-Reflected-Backward algorithm with Linesearch](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20113)
*Fernando Muñoz García,Fernando Roldán*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文针对单调包含问题（最大单调算子+连续算子之和），提出了一种基于前向-反射-后向（FRB）算法的新型线搜索策略。该策略在算子仅为连续（无需局部Lipschitz）时仍保证线搜索终止和算法收敛，且每次迭代只需一次算子求值，解决了现有FRB线搜索对局部Lipschitz条件的依赖以及FBF算法需两次算子求值的不足。数值实验表明该方法在鞍点问题和图像复原中具有竞争力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有求解单调包含问题的算法（如FBF、FRB）存在以下局限：当连续算子仅满足连续性而非Lipschitz或cocoercive时，传统线搜索策略可能无法终止；FBF算法每次迭代需两次算子求值，计算成本高；已有FRB线搜索版本仅对局部Lipschitz算子收敛。因此，需要设计一种对仅连续算子也有效的线搜索策略，同时保持单次算子求值的效率优势。

Method: 提出一种新型线搜索策略嵌入FRB算法框架：通过构造一个可计算的终止准则，确保在算子仅为连续（非Lipschitz）时线搜索有限步内终止；理论证明该线搜索的良定义性和算法收敛性；进一步将算法扩展至包含额外cocoercive和Lipschitz连续算子的情形。

Result: 数值实验结果表明：1）所提FRB线搜索在Lipschitz连续算子场景下能加速数值收敛；2）与线搜索FBF相比，该方法在多个场景下具有竞争力，且因单次算子求值带来显著计算优势。

Conclusion: 提出的FRB线搜索策略克服了现有方法对算子Lipschitz条件的依赖，在仅连续算子下仍保证收敛，同时保持计算效率。该方法为单调包含问题提供了一种更通用且高效的求解方案。

Abstract: In this article, we aim to solve a monotone inclusion problem involving the sum of a maximally monotone operator and a continuous operator. While several algorithms exist to solve this problem when the continuous operator is cocoercive or Lipschitz continuous, they typically require the estimation of the global Lipschitz constant, which can be computationally expensive and often imposes overly restrictive step-sizes. To avoid these limitations and to handle merely continuous operators, linesearch subroutines are employed. A popular method in this context is the forward-backward-forward (FBF) algorithm (also known as Tseng's splitting), which utilizes a linesearch to guarantee convergence. However, a drawback of FBF is that the continuous operator must be evaluated twice per iteration. On the other hand, the forward-reflected-backward (FRB) algorithm proposed by Malitsky and Tam (2020) requires only a single evaluation of the operator per iteration. Although a linesearch version of FRB exists, its convergence is guaranteed only for locally Lipschitz operators; in fact, we present an example demonstrating that this existing linesearch can fail to terminate when the operator is merely continuous. In this work, we propose a novel linesearch strategy for FRB that is well defined and guarantees convergence even when the operator is merely continuous. We also extend the proposed algorithm to handle additional cocoercive and Lipschitz continuous operators. Finally, we provide numerical experiments on saddle-point problems and image restoration. The numerical results show that FRB with the proposed linesearch can accelerate the numerical convergence even when the operator is Lipschitz continuous. In addition, these results show that the proposed method is competitive with linesearch FBF, offering considerable computational advantages in various scenarios.

</details>


### [167] [A Coupled Nonsmooth Dynamical System: Global Well-Posedness, Stability and Sensitivity Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20133)
*Shengda Zeng,Jia Chen,Vo Thanh Phat*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类耦合非光滑动力系统，其中半线性发展方程与由法锥（依赖于时间变化凸集）控制的隐式代数律相耦合。通过变换变量将冻结代数律重构为凸集上的变分不等式，在强伪单调、Lipschitz连续假设下证明了代数响应的唯一性及状态到控制映射的灵敏度估计。利用C₀-半群估计与Bielecki不动点论证，证明了有限时间区间上温和解对的全局存在唯一性及Hadamard适定性，并建立了指数稳定性判据与参数到解映射的连续性。接触力学实例展示了变分不等式公式及投影残差形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有耦合非光滑动力系统的研究中，代数变量通常由显式反馈给出，而实际应用中（如接触力学）代数变量需从状态相关的法锥关系中恢复，缺乏一般性理论框架与分析工具。

Method: 引入变换变量将冻结代数律转化为凸集上的变分不等式；利用强伪单调性、Lipschitz连续性导出灵敏度估计（避免投影-压缩论证）；结合C₀-半群估计与Bielecki不动点定理处理耦合系统；通过加权强单调构造和Lipschitz小条件给出可验证的充分条件。

Result: 证明了代数响应唯一性及状态到控制映射的灵敏度估计；建立了有限时间区间上温和解对的全局存在唯一性与Hadamard适定性；推导了耗散半群情形下的增量指数稳定性判据；证明了参数到解映射对初值和外部参数的连续性；接触力学算例验证了变分不等式公式与投影残差的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的框架无需投影-压缩论证即可处理状态相关法锥耦合的隐式代数律，为接触力学等应用场景提供了理论支撑与数值求解的起点（投影法和牛顿型内层求解器）。

Abstract: This paper studies a coupled nonsmooth dynamical system in which a semilinear evolution equation is coupled with an implicit algebraic law governed by the normal cone to a time-dependent convex set. The main difficulty is that the algebraic variable is not given by an explicit feedback, but must be recovered from a state-dependent normal cone relation. Using a transformed variable, we recast each frozen algebraic law as a variational inequality over a convex set. Under a strongly pseudomonotone, Lipschitz continuous hypothesis, this frozen problem has a unique algebraic response and admits a sensitivity estimate for the state-to-control map without a projection-contraction argument. We also give verifiable sufficient conditions for this hypothesis, including a weighted strongly monotone construction and a standard Lipschitz-smallness condition, and point out that the framework allows strongly pseudomonotone nonmonotone frozen operators. The coupled system is then reduced to a semilinear evolution equation with a single state variable. By combining $C_0$-semigroup estimates with a Bielecki fixed-point argument, we prove global existence and uniqueness of mild solution pairs on finite time intervals and establish Hadamard well-posedness through explicit continuous-dependence estimates. We further derive an incremental exponential stability criterion in the dissipative semigroup regime and prove continuity of the parameter-to-solution map with respect to the initial datum and an external parameter. A reduced contact-mechanics example illustrates the variational inequality formulation and an explicit projection residual that can be used as a starting point for projection- and Newton-type inner solvers after discretization.

</details>


### [168] [Decentralized Online Riemannian Optimization for Strongly Geodesically Convex Functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20316)
*Zhanyuan Cai,Emre Sahinoglu,Shahin Shahrampour*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文研究了黎曼流形上强测地凸损失的分散在线优化，首次实现O(log T)静态遗憾界，并扩展至两点带隙反馈场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有分散黎曼优化方法仅处理一般g-凸损失，未探索强g-凸情形；集中式优化中强g-凸可实现O(log T)遗憾，但衰减步长策略与分散网络误差分析不兼容。

Method: 提出适用于时变调度的通用网络误差分析框架；基于此分析分散在线黎曼梯度下降的遗憾界；采用强次凸性论证处理两点带隙反馈。

Conclusion: 本文填补了分散黎曼优化中强g-凸损失的理论空白，证明了分散设置下亦可达到集中式强凸在线优化的最优遗憾界。

Abstract: We study decentralized online optimization for strongly geodesically convex (strongly g-convex) losses on Riemannian manifolds with bounded sectional curvature, including positively curved manifolds. In centralized Riemannian optimization, strong g-convexity tightens the optimal regret from $O(\sqrt{T})$ to $O(\log T)$, where $T$ is the time horizon; in the decentralized Riemannian setting, however, existing methods address only g-convex losses, leaving the strongly g-convex regime unexplored. One challenge is that the required decaying step size in the centralized regime is incompatible with existing network-error analyses, which typically assume a fixed step size. First, we provide a general network-error analysis for time-varying schedules. Next, we build on this analysis to establish the first $O(\log T)$ static regret bound for decentralized online Riemannian gradient descent, matching the minimax-optimal rate for strongly-convex Euclidean online optimization. Finally, we prove the same $O(\log T)$ regret bound for the two-point bandit feedback setting using novel strong subconvexity arguments for the smoothed versions of the loss functions.

Applications include uniform convergence of limiting and Clarke subdifferentials and finite-sample identification of solutions. ### [171] [Cavitation Acoustic Perturbation Equations: A Computational Framework for Source-Resolved Multiphase Hydroacoustics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19567)
*Zhi Cheng,Rajeev K. Jaiman*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文提出了空化一致性声学扰动框架（CAPE），将空化物理直接嵌入声学方程，通过汽相质量传递、混合物可压缩性和压力率效应的统一建模，实现了空化流动中声波产生与传播的预测。在一维波传播问题上验证后，应用于圆柱和NACA水翼空化流，揭示了非空化时的偶极子辐射和空化时的单极子/几何调制辐射，并识别了涡脱落、空泡脱落和溃灭对应的源项频率特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统声学扰动方程仅适用于单相或弱可压缩流，无法处理空化流动中汽液两相转变带来的复杂声源机制，亟需发展能够直接嵌入空化物理的声学建模方法。

Method: 提出空化声学扰动方程（CAPE），将汽相质量传递、混合物可压缩性和压力率效应统一纳入声学扰动框架；采用完美匹配层吸收边界；通过一维波传播问题进行验证，并在圆柱绕流和NACA水翼空化流中应用。

Result: 非空化工况呈现与非定常载荷相关的偶极子辐射；空化工况呈现由体积相变引起的单极子或几何调制辐射；源项分析识别出涡脱落、空泡脱落和溃 collapse 对应的特征频率；相变项提供单极子源的直接体积贡献，溃 collapse 事件通过压力率源放大体现。

Conclusion: CAPE框架将声学扰动方法扩展至空化多相流，为海洋和水力工程中的水声预测、声源定位和机理分析提供了高效工具。

Abstract: This work develops a cavitation-consistent acoustic perturbation framework for predicting sound generation and propagation in cavitating flows. Unlike conventional acoustic perturbation equations for single-phase or weakly compressible flows, the proposed formulation embeds cavitation physics directly into the acoustic equations. The cavitation acoustic perturbation equations (CAPE) incorporate vapor mass transfer, mixture compressibility, and pressure-rate effects within a unified formulation, allowing cavitation-induced noise sources to be resolved in the computational domain. The numerical framework is verified using one-dimensional wave-propagation problems. The solutions become insensitive to further mesh and time-step refinement, the perfectly matched layer suppresses boundary reflections, and the predicted attenuation over a range of source frequencies follows Stokes' sound attenuation law. The framework is then applied to cavitating flow past a circular cylinder and a NACA hydrofoil. The non-cavitating benchmark shows dipole-like radiation associated with unsteady loading, whereas cavitating cases exhibit monopole-like or geometry-modulated radiation caused by volumetric phase change. Source-term analyses identify tonal frequencies associated with vortex shedding, cavity shedding, and collapse-induced excitation. The phase-change terms provide a direct volumetric contribution to the monopole-like source, while localized collapse events appear through amplification of the pressure-rate source. The proposed framework extends acoustic perturbation methods to cavitating multiphase flows and provides an efficient tool for hydroacoustic prediction, source localization, and mechanism analysis in marine and hydraulic applications.

</details>


### [172] [Elastohydrodynamic instability of a spinning elastic disk](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19561)
*Sifan Yin,Paul R. Kaneelil,L. Mahadevan*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文研究旋转弹性薄圆盘在粘性流体中的屈曲不稳定性。通过耦合福普尔-冯·卡门方程与冯·卡门旋流理论，发现流体剪切力可导致圆盘失稳，产生周期性鞍形屈曲模态和反向行波，屈曲波数随旋转张力增大而增加。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究粘性流体中旋转弹性薄盘的失稳机制，特别是离心刚化与流体剪切之间的竞争关系如何导致屈曲。

Method: 将线性化福普尔-冯·卡门方程与经典冯·卡门旋流的剪切应力耦合，构建弹性流体动力学稳定性问题，通过线性稳定性分析求解。

Result: 发现了由两个无量纲控制参数（离心刚化与流体剪切）决定的屈曲阈值，屈曲模态为方位角周期性的鞍形模式，波数随旋转张力增加而增大；屈曲构型还支持比材料框架旋转更慢的逆行行波。

Conclusion: 揭示了流体剪切力使旋转弹性结构失稳的简单机制，为理解弹性结构与粘性流体耦合系统中的不稳定性提供了理论基础。

Abstract: A soft thin elastic disk spinning in a viscous fluid experiences centrifugal tension generated by rotation together with viscous shear generated by the surrounding flow. While the former stabilizes the flat state, the latter can destabilize it. We combine the linearized Föppl-von Kármán equations for a rotating elastic disk with the shear stresses arising from the classical von Kármán swirling flow to derive an elastohydrodynamic stability problem. Linear stability analysis identifies the onset of buckling in terms of two dimensionless control parameters measuring centrifugal stiffening and fluid-induced shear. Above threshold the disk buckles into azimuthally periodic saddle-like modes whose wavenumber increases with increasing rotational tension. The buckled configuration also supports retrograde traveling waves that rotate more slowly than the material frame. These results identify a simple mechanism whereby fluid shear destabilizes rotating elastic structures.

### [173] [The spectral picture of self-similar collapse in the Constantin-Lax-Majda equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19762)
*Jie Xu*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文对Constantin-Lax-Majda (CLM)方程自相似坍塌剖面的谱性质进行了完整刻画，在a=0情形下证明了：本质谱仅包含竖直直线{Re λ = -1/2}，点谱仅为{0,1}（对应标度与时间平移对称模态），移除对称模态后谱隙为1/2；通过有界转移映射在加权空间上精确计算了线性半群及其衰减率e^{-τ/2}；揭示了实现差异导致的谱结构区别；对a>0情形给出了条件性双线包含关系，并计算了分支c_l(a)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立CLM方程自相似坍塌剖面的完整谱理论，特别是实现依赖的谱结构，以理解非线性聚焦过程中的线性稳定性和衰减率。

Method: 将线性化算子L_0实现为原点H^2空间上的闭算子，使用对数加宽Weyl序列定位本质谱，利用显式Hardy-Mellin预解式有界性证明谱空隙，通过有界转移映射在加权空间中计算半群衰减率，并分析不同实现（H^2与最大L^2实现）之间的谱差异。

Result: 在a=0时：本质谱为{Re λ = -1/2}；点谱为{0,1}；移除对称模态后在X空间上谱隙为1/2；在加权空间中精确半群衰减率为e^{-τ/2}；H^2实现消除了最大L^2实现中的条带谱污染。对a>0：证明了条件性双线包含关系，重新计算了分支c_l(a)及标度相关指数s^*(a)。

Conclusion: 谱隙的存在（1/2）并不直接在原始X范数下给出衰减率，揭示了非正规算子的谱理论与半群衰减行为之间的复杂关系；实现了对坍塌剖面本征谱的实现依赖谱结构的完整刻画。

Abstract: We give a spectral description of the self-similar collapse profile of the Constantin-Lax-Majda (CLM) equation, the $a=0$ anchor of the generalized family $w_t + a\,u\,w_x = u_x\,w$, $u_x = Hw$. Linearizing about the exact profile $Ω(y) = -y/(y^2+1/4)$ and realizing $L_0$ as a closed operator on the origin-$H^2$ space, we prove three things at $a=0$. Its essential spectrum meets the closed half-plane $\{\mathrm{Re}\,λ\ge -1/2\}$ in the single vertical line $\{\mathrm{Re}\,λ= -1/2\}$: the line is placed by a log-widening Weyl sequence, and an explicit Hardy-Mellin resolvent bound constructively empties the rest of the half-plane apart from $0$ and $1$. Its full point spectrum over $\mathbb{C}$, on the odd realization, is exactly $\{0,1\}$, the scaling and time-shift symmetry modes, with no embedded eigenvalues; removing these by the standard modulation leaves a spectral gap of $1/2$ on $X$. The linear semigroup and its exact decay rate $e^{-τ/2}$ are computed in closed form, but on a weighted space of the conjugated variable reached from $X$ by a bounded transfer map; we keep the two separate, since $L_0$ is non-normal and a spectral gap does not by itself give a decay rate in the $X$ norm. A realization dichotomy identifies the in-strip smear of generic discretizations as the faithful spectrum of the maximal $L^2$ realization, which origin-$H^2$ removes. For $a>0$ we prove a conditional two-line inclusion for each admissible smooth focusing profile, recompute the branch $c_l(a)$ of Lushnikov, Silantyev, and Siegel as a cross-check, and record the formal scaling-relevance exponent $s^*(a) = 1/c_l(a)$, below which fractional dissipation is asymptotically subdominant in self-similar variables for fixed sufficiently regular data. The contribution is the realization-dependent spectral picture of the collapse profile itself.

### [174] [Sidewall effects on the onset of interfacial Holmboe waves in stratified exchange flows at high Schmidt number](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19565)
*Guilherme Siqueira de Aquino,Metten M. de Lange,Adrien Lefauve,Matias Duran-Matute*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文通过长管道、尖锐界面渐近理论，推导出三维层流交换流的解析解，并定义了一个考虑侧壁摩擦的调整弗劳德数Fr*，该单一参数统一了驱动力和几何约束对有效层流交换流的影响。结合线性稳定性分析、直接数值模拟和已有实验，证明波的发生可由Fr*的近似常数临界值准确预测。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用长管道、尖锐界面的渐近理论推导三维层流交换流解析解，考虑侧壁摩擦效应；用该解参数化侧壁阻力得到宽度平均模型；进行线性稳定性分析和高施密特数直接数值模拟。

Conclusion: 这些发现为波的发生提供了预测判据，调和了不同实验配置之间长期存在的差异，并确立了侧向约束作为分层剪切流中层流交换向波动驱动混合转变的基本控制因素。

Abstract: Predicting the onset of interfacial instabilities is central to understanding turbulent mixing in natural and engineered stratified shear flows. Here, we study the onset of travelling Holmboe waves in confined exchange flows along a slope. Earlier stratified inclined duct experiments have mapped this transition, and stability analyses based on measured or prescribed profiles have explained their emergence. However, a predictive criterion linking forcing, geometry, base flow, and wave onset was still lacking. We closed this gap with a long-duct, sharp-interface asymptotic theory for the three-dimensional laminar exchange flow, including the effects of sidewall friction. The resulting analytical solution naturally identifies a confinement-adjusted Froude number, $Fr^*$, which unifies the effects of forcing and confinement into a single measure of the effective laminar exchange flow. Using this solution to parameterise sidewall drag in a practical width-averaged model, we perform linear stability analyses and numerical simulations at high Schmidt number. Together, linear stability analysis, direct numerical simulations, and existing experiments across a range of duct widths show that wave onset is accurately predicted by an approximately constant critical value of $Fr^*$. Deviations arise only in very narrow ducts, where sidewalls influence instability not only by modifying the laminar exchange flow but also by directly damping perturbations and delaying wave onset. These findings provide a predictive criterion for wave onset, reconcile long-standing discrepancies among experimental configurations, and establish lateral confinement as a fundamental control on the transition from laminar exchange to wave-driven mixing in stratified shear flows.

Over the past decade, computational modeling has emerged as a powerful tool to advance cardiovascular research by enabling detailed, patient-specific studies of cardiac physiology and pathology. svMultiPhysics is an open-source, parallel finite element solver written in C++ specifically designed for multiphysics cardiovascular problems. It provides a unified framework for simulating the partial differential equations that govern solid mechanics, fluid dynamics, diffusion, and cardiac electrophysiology. These equations can be solved independently or in a coupled fashion, allowing researchers to investigate interactions between physical processes in a modular yet integrated way. The solver's main strength lies in its ability to seamlessly couple multiple physics modules, enabling the study of complex, highly nonlinear systems. For example, svMultiPhysics can capture the interplay between cardiac electrophysiology, myocardial tissue mechanics, and blood flow dynamics, processes that are essential to understanding vascular and cardiac physiology and function in health and disease. Preliminary GPU-enabled simulations show up to approximately $30\times$ wall-clock speedup for selected linear solver configurations over CPU-based simulations. Abstract: When a sphere crosses an air-water interface it can entrain a significant volume of air, a process relevant to numerous naval, industrial, and environmental settings. While air entrainment through sphere impact onto quiescent baths has been extensively studied, real-world interfaces are inherently unsteady, and the influence of surface waves is less understood. In this Letter, we systematically investigate the effect of interfacial geometry on the air entrained by impacting hydrophobic spheres onto an axisymmetric wavefield. By analyzing the resulting cavity across a wide parameter space, including wave phase, driving amplitude, and frequency, we reveal that local interface deformation dramatically alters air entrainment. This effect is driven by a geometric modulation of the splash curtain, which shifts the transition between cavity closure modes. We demonstrate that the influence of the waves is fully described by the local wave slope at the radius of the sphere, which alongside the Weber number We and Bond number Bo, establishes a foundational parametric framework for predicting air entrainment and cavity metrics across highly dynamic, real-world surfaces like the open ocean.

### [178] [Theoretical development of an operational wave-induced ice erosion model through laboratory experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20118)
*Wenjun Lu,Behnam Ghadimi,Dominique Mouaze,Marianne Font,Rémi Lambert,Harvey Goodwin,Widar Weizhi Wang,Raed Lubbad,Sveinung Løset*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文重构了White (1980)基于粗糙壁面参数的波浪诱导垂直冰面融化模型，明确其湍流摩擦闭合采用Jonsson隐式关系及Lambert-W解，并将模型推广到深度分辨的融化率剖面。通过两个淡冰水槽实验标定闭合系数alpha，获得与水线系数接近的结果，但未能独立验证White的原始值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: White (1980)的粗糙壁面参数化方案被广泛用于冰山和海岸侵蚀模型，但其闭合链记录不完整且常用表达式仅定义在水线处，缺乏深度解析的融化率分布。

Method: 重构White模型，引入Jonsson隐式关系的Lambert-W解作为粗糙湍流波动摩擦闭合，利用水平轨道速度作为代表尺度并引入无量纲系数alpha处理剩余闭合不确定性。通过两个淡冰单色波浪水槽实验（周期1.54s和0.87s）标定alpha。

Result: 水线系数重构值为3.0×10^-4（White合成速度定义）和2.09×10^-4（alpha=1参考选择），均未复现White的1.46×10^-4。实验标定alpha为0.684和0.612（相对差异约11%），对应有效水线系数1.43×10^-4和1.28×10^-4，接近White值但非独立验证。拟合剖面再现了波谷以下的深度依赖性，但近表面偏差揭示了间歇淹没、局部波浪冲击和不确定热强迫等未解析效应。

Conclusion: 成功重构并扩展了White模型到深度分辨剖面，实验标定获得与White原始值接近的有效水线系数，但模型在近表面区域仍存在未解决的物理效应，需进一步改进。

Abstract: Wave-induced melting of vertical ice fronts is represented in several operational iceberg and coastal-erosion models by the rough-wall parameterization of White (1980), whose closure chain is incompletely documented and whose commonly used compact expression is stated at the waterline. We reconstruct the formulation, specify the rough-turbulent wave-friction closure using Jonsson's implicit relation and its Lambert-W solution, and extend the model to a depth-resolved melt-rate profile under linear wave kinematics. Because the horizontal and vertical orbital-velocity components are linked, we use the horizontal component as a convenient representative scale and introduce a dimensionless coefficient alpha for the remaining closure uncertainty. The reconstruction gives a waterline coefficient of 3.0 x 10^-4 with White's resultant-velocity definition and 2.09 x 10^-4 for the reference choice alpha = 1; neither reproduces White's published 1.46 x 10^-4 directly. Two monochromatic wave-flume experiments with freshwater ice are then used to calibrate alpha from profiles below the wave trough. The full Lambert-W friction coefficient is used in this calibration. Best-fit values are 0.684 and 0.612 for periods of 1.54 and 0.87 s, respectively, a relative difference of approximately 11%. Their corresponding effective waterline coefficients, 1.43 x 10^-4 and 1.28 x 10^-4, are close to White's published value but do not constitute an independent validation. The fitted profiles reproduce the observed depth dependence below the trough, while deviations near the surface expose unresolved effects of intermittent submergence, local wave impact, and uncertain thermal forcing.

### [179] [A High-Order Flux Reconstruction Actuator-Line Framework for Rotating-Blade Aerodynamics on Fixed Cartesian Grids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20347)
*Abdullah Al Imran,Meilin Yu*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将高精度通量重构/校正过程重构（FR/CPR）求解器与旋转致动线模型（ALM）耦合的框架，在固定笛卡尔网格上模拟旋转叶片空气动力学。通过各向同性高斯核在叶片附着坐标系中投影体作用力源项来表征叶片载荷，无需解析叶片几何。以垂直轴风力涡轮机（VAWTs）为验证对象，融合改进的Boeing-Vertol动态失速模型捕捉非定常升力和阻力。推导了中等粗糙网格下高斯投影核的网格分辨率准则，并提出双多流管（DMST）修正以恢复物理入流。在弦雷诺数Re_c~3.6×10^5下进行变叶尖速比仿真，与实验近尾流测量和LES-ALM结果吻合良好，最优工况下功率系数预测与高保真三维LES-ALM数据偏差在6%以内，成功捕捉动态失速、方位角叶片载荷、升力迟滞及特征尾流结构。该FR/CPR-ALM框架为VAWT分析提供了一种精确、计算高效的几何无关方法，适用于参数化研究和大型风能应用。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: This work couples a high-order flux reconstruction/correction procedure via reconstruction (FR/CPR) solver with a rotating actuator-line model (ALM) to simulate rotating-blade aerodynamics on fixed Cartesian grids. Blade loading is represented by volumetric body force source terms projected through an isotropic Gaussian kernel in a blade-attached frame, eliminating the need to resolve blade geometry. Vertical-axis wind turbines (VAWTs) serve as the demonstration configuration, with a modified Boeing-Vertol dynamic stall model incorporated to capture unsteady lift and drag. A mesh-resolution criterion for the Gaussian projection kernel on reasonably coarse meshes is derived. It shows that cost-effective coarse meshes can operate in a mesh-controlled regime with negligible induction feedback, motivating a Double Multiple Streamtube (DMST) correction to recover the physical inflow. Simulations are carried out over a range of tip-speed ratios at a chord-based Reynolds number of Re_c ~ 3.6 x 10^5. The framework is validated against experimental near-wake measurements and previously reported LES-ALM results, and the mean wake profile shows good agreement. The predicted power-coefficient curve matches high-fidelity three-dimensional LES-ALM data to within 6% around the optimal VAWT operation conditions. The framework also captures the regime-dependent influence of dynamic stall, azimuthal blade loading, lift hysteresis, and characteristic wake structures. These results demonstrate that the FR/CPR-ALM framework provides an accurate and computationally efficient geometry-free approach for VAWT analysis, making it well suited for parametric studies and large-scale wind energy applications.

### [180] [Hard Guarantees at a Measured Price: Entropy-Stable Learned Finite Volumes for Compressible Flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20171)
*Denis Gueyffier*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种面向非结构化网格上二维欧拉方程的可学习有限体积格式，该格式通过构造保证物理可容许性（无负密度/压力），并具有熵稳定的内部通量。在等网格分辨率下，未学习骨架（两个学习头关闭）最强；在等计算成本下，学习在壁面边界案例上获益（+10.8%），但周期案例增益波动（+10%到-12%）；保证方案完成全部36次 rollout，零负事件。通过尺度不变输入和比熵下限，在推理时修复了马赫数外推的弱点。空间门控策略（仅壁面附近激活学习头）超越了骨架和修正臂，并零迁移到新壁面几何。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的可学习求解器通常只在等网格分辨率下与经典方法比较，未考虑计算成本，且无法保证解在物理上可容许（如出现负密度或压力）。本文旨在填补这一空白：构建一个在构造上保证物理可容许性、具有熵稳定性质的可学习格式，并在等计算成本协议下系统评估其实际收益。

Method: 1) 在非结构化网格上构建可学习有限体积格式，包含两个可学习头（通量和限制器），并嵌入保证机制（熵稳定内部通量 + 物理可容许性约束）；2) 设计严格评估协议：冻结阈值、证伪条款、阴性对照、因子分解（分离学习头与骨架）、等成本比较；3) 提出推理时修复方法：尺度不变网络输入 + 特定比熵下限（无需重训练）；4) 提出空间门控策略：仅在壁面附近激活学习头。

Result: 1) 因子分解核心结果：未学习骨架（两个头关闭）在所有周期算例上等网格最强；2) 等成本比较：学习仅在未见过的壁面边界类型上稳健获益（+10.8%），周期算例增益随评估波动（+10%到-12%）；骨架的等成本增益符号永不改变；3) 保证方案完成36/36 rollout，零负事件，开销1.74x/步；4) 推理时修复：修正臂在马赫数算例上超越无约束臂，在未见壁面上超越骨架；5) 空间门控：仅壁面附近激活学习头，同时超越骨架和修正臂，零迁移到新壁面几何。

Conclusion: 可学习求解器的物理可容许性保证在工程可靠性上具有重要价值（零负事件），但学习在泛化边界条件时增益有限且易翻转。骨架（未学习基础格式）在等成本下最稳健。空间门控策略（仅在需要处启用学习）提供了最佳的精度-稳健性权衡，并具有几何迁移能力。未来工作应关注计算效率提升（1.74x开销）和更广泛的外推场景验证。

Abstract: Learned solvers for compressible flow are usually compared to classical methods at equal mesh resolution rather than at equal computational cost, and they typically offer no guarantee that their solutions remain physically admissible. We present a learned finite volume scheme for the two-dimensional Euler equations on unstructured meshes, admissible by construction and with an entropy-stable interior flux. We evaluate it under protocols fixed before any computation: frozen thresholds, falsification clauses, negative controls, a factor decomposition of the learned components, and an iso-cost comparison against the refined classical baseline. The decomposition produced the central result: the guarantee machinery alone, with both learned heads switched off (the unlearned skeleton), is the strongest scheme at equal mesh on every periodic case. At equal wall-clock cost the picture inverts into a map. Learning pays robustly only on the wall case whose boundary-condition type it never saw (10.8%). Its periodic gains flip sign with the evaluation draw (+10% on one held-out case, -12% on the hardest). The skeleton is the only method whose iso-cost gain never changes sign, at a measured overhead of 1.74x per step. The guaranteed variant completes 36 of 36 rollouts, Mach extrapolation and unseen wall included, with zero negativity events. We fix the guaranteed scheme's one remaining out-of-distribution weakness, Mach extrapolation, at inference time: with scale-invariant network inputs, a specific-entropy floor, and no retraining, the corrected arm overtakes the unconstrained arm on one Mach case, cuts its deficit on the other by a third, passes the skeleton on the unseen wall, and keeps the guarantee. A spatial gate closes the loop: activating the heads only near the walls beats both the skeleton and the corrected arm, and transfers unchanged to a second wall geometry.

### [181] [Information Transport and Observability in Compressible Aerodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20177)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 压力测量虽能提供可压缩空气动力学流动的直接稀疏观测，但隐式气动参数如何通过流场传输并被编码到这些观测中的机制尚不清楚，缺乏定量的可观测性分析框架。

Method: 采用可微分的激波捕获浸没边界求解器，通过自动微分传播整个非定常流场解的梯度，引入基于自动微分的可观测性度量，量化稀疏压力测量对未知气动参数的敏感性，并识别有信息量的传感位置。

Result: 气动信息在流场中非均匀传输，产生局部高可观测性区域；可观测性与可学习性相关但不同——高可观测性探针通常利于参数恢复，但最高可观测性探针并非始终最有效；流态和翼型几何显著影响可观测性分布与逆学习收敛行为。

Conclusion: 建立了理解稀疏测量中气动信息编码的定量框架，展示了自动微分在可观测性分析、信息性传感器选择和空气动力学逆分析中的潜力。

Abstract: Pressure measurements provide sparse but direct observations of compressible aerodynamic flows, yet how information about hidden aerodynamic parameters is transported through the flow and encoded in these observations remains poorly understood. Here, we investigate information transport and observability in compressible aerodynamics using a differentiable shock-capturing immersed-boundary solver. By propagating gradients through the full unsteady flow solution, an automatic-differentiation-based observability metric is introduced to quantify the sensitivity of sparse pressure measurements to unknown aerodynamic parameters and identify informative sensing locations for inverse learning. The results reveal that aerodynamic information is transported non-uniformly through the flow field, producing localized regions of high observability. Inverse-learning experiments further demonstrate that observability and learnability are related but distinct concepts: although highly observable probes generally facilitate accurate parameter recovery, the highest-observability probe is not consistently the most effective for parameter inference. Furthermore, both the flow regime and the airfoil geometry substantially influence the distribution of observability and the convergence behavior of inverse learning. These findings establish a quantitative framework for understanding how aerodynamic information is encoded in sparse measurements and demonstrate the potential of automatic differentiation for observability analysis, informative sensor selection, and aerodynamic inverse analysis.

Their combined analysis provides a physically meaningful classification of breather regimes beyond the conventional focusing condition of the nonlinear Schrödinger equation. Reconstruction of the physical interfacial profile establishes a quantitative relation between nonlinear wave deformation and the contribution of the bound second harmonic, making it possible to identify the range of applicability of the weakly nonlinear approximation. Representative regimes from different modulational instability regions are analyzed to demonstrate the influence of resonance and focusing boundaries on breather characteristics and interfacial wave profiles. The proposed approach provides a direct link between the mathematical description of Akhmediev breathers and their physical interpretation and can be extended to other localized solutions of the nonlinear Schrödinger equation and to a broad class of stratified hydrodynamic systems.

### [183] [A formal log(Re)-cost framework for the engineering turbulence problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20199)
*Jiaqi Li,Robert F. Kunz,George Huang,Xiang I. A. Yang*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 湍流问题长期面临预测精度与计算成本之间的权衡。实际工程算法要求计算成本增长不超过O(N)，而湍流问题规模由雷诺数Re决定。现有方法难以同时满足精度与O(N)复杂度要求，亟需一种能在可承受计算成本下实现准确预测的框架。

Method: 采用多保真、物理约束、数据驱动框架：通过场反演和机器学习增强Spalart-Allmaras模型，使用约束公式保留壁面律；在低雷诺数（高保真数据可负担）下训练，在高雷诺数下部署；利用平均流对齐网格、固定展向分辨率、稳态求解器线性成本等条件，实现计算复杂度分析。

Conclusion: 该框架在理论复杂度上达到O(log(Re))，满足实际工程要求；通过物理约束和数据驱动的结合，实现了跨雷诺数的准确预测和鲁棒外推，为湍流建模提供了一种高效可行的解决方案。

Abstract: In fluid engineering, the turbulence problem is the longstanding challenge of obtaining accurate predictions of engineering quantities at affordable computational cost. Viewed through computational complexity, a practical algorithm requires cost growth no worse than $O(N)$, where $N$ denotes problem size. For turbulent flows, the problem size may be approximated by the number of dynamically relevant scales and hence by the Reynolds number $Re$. We propose a multi-fidelity, physics-constrained, data-driven framework designed to meet this criterion under stated assumptions. We augment the Spalart--Allmaras model through field inversion and machine learning using a constrained formulation that preserves the law of the wall. The model is trained at a low Reynolds number, where high-fidelity data are affordable, and deployed at higher Reynolds numbers. For a mean-flow-aligned grid in a wall-bounded flow, fixed spanwise resolution, and steady-solver cost linear in grid-point count, the low-fidelity RANS prediction scales as $O(\log(Re))$. The high-fidelity calculation and learning stage each contribute $O(Re^0)$ relative to the target Reynolds number, giving an overall formal cost of $O(\log(Re))$. In plane channel flow, a model trained at $Re_τ=1000$ corrects the wake-layer error of the baseline model and retains the improvement at $Re_τ=5200$. In the periodic hill, a model trained at $Re_b=5600$ is tested at $Re_b=10595$, $19000$, and $37000$. The constrained formulation preserves separation and recovery behavior as Reynolds number increases, yields the lowest root-mean-square error across all tests, and exhibits nearly Reynolds-number-independent error, indicating robust extrapolation.

### [184] [Bayesian finite element regression for vascular flow reconstruction with quantified uncertainty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20224)
*Cem Gormezano,Shawn Shadden*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文提出一种贝叶斯有限元回归框架，用于从含噪、欠分辨的血流速度观测中重建稳态三维速度场和压力场，并量化不确定性。该方法无需离线训练数据，通过最大熵原理构建物理信息先验，结合泰勒-胡德有限元基函数，通过最大后验估计求解大规模稀疏非线性最小二乘问题（压力可解析消去、无滑移壁面精确约束、梯度计算无需伴随/自动微分），并利用拉普拉斯近似量化不确定性。在患者-specific的脑动脉瘤、主动脉瘤和主动脉缩窄几何上，该方法重建速度/压力优于三次插值，与PINN相当，且壁面剪切应力恢复更准确。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从欠分辨、含噪的血流测量中重建精确的速度和压力场是一个病态逆问题，主要难点在于入口和出口边界条件未知。现有方法（如插值、PINN）在不确定性量化和计算效率上存在不足，亟需一种无需离线训练数据、可量化不确定性的重建方法。

Method: (1) 将速度、压力场表示为泰勒-胡德有限元基函数；(2) 基于最大熵原理构建节点自由度的物理信息先验；(3) 结合噪声模型似然，得到后验分布，其MAP估计给出重建结果；(4) MAP估计通过求解大规模稀疏非线性最小二乘问题计算，其中压力被解析消去、无滑移壁面精确施加、梯度计算无需前向/伴随求解或自动微分；(5) 利用拉普拉斯近似量化后验不确定性，并传播至压降、流量、壁面剪切应力等临床相关量。

Result: 在患者-specific脑动脉瘤、主动脉瘤和主动脉缩窄几何上，该方法重建速度/压力精度优于三次插值，与PINN相当；在感兴趣区域的壁面剪切应力恢复上优于两种对比方法。

Conclusion: 贝叶斯有限元回归框架能够有效从欠分辨含噪观测中重建血流速度/压力场并量化不确定性，无需离线训练数据，在临床相关量的恢复上表现出优势。

Abstract: Reconstructing accurate velocity and pressure fields from under-resolved noisy measurements of blood flow is an ill-posed inverse problem due to unknown inlet and outlet boundary conditions. We present a Bayesian finite element regression framework that reconstructs steady three-dimensional velocity and pressure fields, with quantified uncertainty, from noisy velocity observations without offline training data. We represent velocity and pressure fields in Taylor-Hood finite element basis functions, and construct physics-informed priors on the nodal degrees of freedom from maximum-entropy principles. Combined with a likelihood specified by a noise-model, this yields a posterior whose maximum-a-posteriori estimate (MAP) gives velocity and pressure reconstructions. The MAP estimate is computed by solving a large-scale sparse nonlinear least-squares problem where pressure is eliminated analytically, no-slip walls are enforced exactly, and gradient is computed without forward/adjoint solves or automatic differentiation. A Laplace approximation of the posterior quantifies the uncertainties in our reconstructions and propagates them to clinically relevant quantities of interest including, pressure drop, flow rates, and wall shear stress. On patient-specific cerebral aneurysm, aortic aneurysm, and aortic coarctation geometries, the method reconstructs velocity and pressure more accurately than tricubic interpolation and comparably to a PINN, while recovering region-of-interest wall shear stress more accurately than both.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统数值求解器生成三维热流体场的训练数据需要大量计算和存储资源，成本高昂。

Method: 训练注意力图神经网络，以有限体积法（FVM）残差作为损失函数，直接在网格上评估残差，无需任何标注数据。

Result: 在稳态基准测试中，FVM损失模型全场归一化均方根误差（nRMSE）为2.3-2.8%，与CFD参考结果高度一致；在参数化瞬态案例中，该模型精度优于有监督基线，且完全避免了数据生成成本。

Conclusion: FVM残差可以为神经替代模型提供实用的训练信号，降低模型开发成本。

Abstract: Neural surrogates are widely used in scientific machine learning for fast prediction of three-dimensional (3D) thermo-fluid fields. However, generating training data using conventional numerical solvers often incurs substantial computational and storage costs. We propose to train an attention graph neural network by minimizing the finite-volume method (FVM) residuals of the governing equations. These residuals are evaluated directly on the mesh, requiring no labeled data. We evaluate the trained surrogates against computational fluid dynamics (CFD) references and a data-supervised baseline across four scenarios. On the two steady-state benchmarks, the FVM-loss model achieves an all-field normalized root-mean-square error (nRMSE) of 2.3-2.8%. It demonstrates close agreement with the CFD references, including the buoyancy-energy coupling. On the two parametric transient cases, the FVM-loss model outperforms the supervised baseline in terms of accuracy, while avoiding the data-generation cost entirely. These results indicate that the FVM loss can provide a practical training signal for neural surrogates and reduce the model development cost.

</details>

### [186] [On arrangements of plane real quartics with respect to three lines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19457)
*S. Yu. Orevkov*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文完成了光滑实代数或实伪全纯四次曲线与三条直线在“四边形的每个卵形与直线之并集相交”条件下的相互位置分类。发现一种排列在伪全纯意义下可实现，但在代数意义下不可实现，可通过不规则三角剖分的组合贴补构造，这是首个组合贴补产生与坐标轴相对排列代数不可实现的PL曲线的例子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 完成Maletto近期预印本中启动的关于实四次曲线与三条直线相互位置的分类工作，特别关注代数可实现性与伪全纯可实现性之间的差异。

Method: 采用组合贴补（combinatorial patchworking）方法，在不规则三角剖分上构造PL曲线，并与代数实现进行对比分析。

Result: 给出了完整的分类结果；发现一种排列是伪全纯可实现但代数不可实现的；通过不规则三角剖分的组合贴补首次构造出与坐标轴相对排列代数不可实现的PL曲线。

Conclusion: 实代数曲线与实伪全纯曲线在排列分类上存在差异，组合贴补方法可以产生代数上无法实现的排列，扩展了对实代数曲线可实现性边界的认识。

Abstract: We complete the classification of mutual arrangements of a smooth real algebraic or real pseudoholomorphic quartic curve and three lines under condition that each oval of the quartic intersects the union of the lines. This classification was started in a recent preprint by Maletto. There is one arrangement which is realizable pseudoholomorphically but not algebraically. It can be constructed in different ways, in particular, by a combinatorial patchworking on an irregular triangulation. This is the first example of a combinatorial patchworking which produces a PL curve in $RP^2$ whose arrangement relative to the coordinate axes is algebraically unrealizable.

Abstract: We study the positive Grassmannian through the lens of algebraic statistics. A closed formula is presented for the maximum likelihood degree of the Grassmannian of lines. We conjecture that the probability simplex contains a unique local maximum, and we present computational evidence for this.

### [188] [Derived representation schemes with arbitrary coefficients and associative smoothness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19654)
*Guanyu Li*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文研究了以任意有限维代数为系数的表示同调与结合代数的光滑性之间的关系，证明了有限生成形式光滑代数的更高阶表示同调消失，并发现任意系数相较于矩阵系数能提供更严格的光滑性检验。对于有限维代数，任意系数的表示同调完全刻画了形式光滑性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索表示同调（representation homology）是否能作为结合代数光滑性（associative smoothness）的同伦论刻画，验证推广的Kontsevich-Rosenberg原理是否成立。

Method: 以任意有限维代数为系数的表示同调为工具，研究有限生成形式光滑代数的同调性质，通过比较矩阵系数与任意系数的检测能力来证明后者的严格性，并对有限维代数情况给出刻画定理。

Result: (1) 有限生成形式光滑代数的更高阶表示同调（任意有限维系数）为零；(2) 任意系数比矩阵系数能检测更多非光滑情形；(3) 对有限维代数，任意系数的表示同调完全刻画形式光滑性。

Conclusion: 表示同调（任意有限维系数）有望成为结合代数光滑性的同伦论特征，为推广Kontsevich-Rosenberg原理提供了支持证据。

Abstract: We study associative smoothness through representation homology with coefficients in arbitrary finite-dimensional algebras. We prove that the higher representation homology of a finitely generated formally smooth algebra with arbitrary finite-dimensional coefficients vanishes. We further show that allowing arbitrary coefficients yields a strictly stronger smoothness test: suitable non-matrix coefficients detect nonsmoothness in situations where matrix coefficients do not. These results raise the question of whether representation homology with arbitrary coefficients furnishes a homotopical characterization of associative smoothness in the spirit of the derived Kontsevich-Rosenberg principle. For finite-dimensional algebras, we prove that representation homology with arbitrary coefficients completely characterizes formal smoothness, providing supporting evidence for this philosophy.

### [191] [Lipschitz embeddings of algebraic curves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20111)
*Zbigniew Jelonek,Gustavo Menani,Maria Michalska*

TL;DR: 本文证明实代数曲线的内Lipschitz分类等价于$\mathbb{R}^3$中具有LNE连通分支的实代数曲线的外Lipschitz分类，并为每条实仿射代数曲线构造了与之双有理等价的LNE模型，同时指出该结论在复范畴中不成立。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过理论分析和构造性证明，研究实代数曲线的Lipschitz分类，构造LNE模型并验证其与原始曲线的双有理等价性，最后通过反例说明该结论在复范畴中的失效。

Result: 成功证明了内Lipschitz分类与外Lipschitz分类在$\mathbb{R}^3$中具有LNE连通分支的实代数曲线上的等价性；为每条实仿射代数曲线找到了一个LNE模型，且该模型与原始曲线双有理等价；证明了该结论在复范畴中不成立。

Conclusion: 实代数曲线的Lipschitz分类可通过LNE模型简化，且内、外分类在特定条件下等价，但该框架无法直接推广到复代数曲线。

Abstract: We show that inner Lipschitz classification of real algebraic curves is equivalent to outer Lipschitz classification in $\mathbb{R}^3$ of real algebraic curves with LNE connected components. ### [192] [Connected components of real loci in moduli spaces of vector and Higgs bundles over a Klein surface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20161)
*Florent Schaffhauser,Tommaso Scognamiglio*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文利用规范理论方法，研究了黎曼曲面上反全纯对合诱导的实结构下，半稳定向量丛模空间实连通分支的数量，并将其推广到Higgs丛模空间以及相关超凯勒商中某些Brane的拓扑研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解实代数几何和规范理论中模空间的拓扑结构，特别是实向量丛和Higgs丛模空间的连通分支计数问题，以及其在超凯勒商和Brane理论中的应用。

Method: 采用规范理论方法（gauge-theoretic approach），通过分析反全纯对合在模空间上的诱导作用，计算实点集（real locus）的连通分支数。

Result: 当基曲线有实点时，四元数向量丛存在于偶秩偶度情形，但实模空间连通分支数仍与实Picard簇相等；当基曲线无实点且秩与度不互素时，实模空间连通分支数可能小于实Picard簇的连通分支数。并将结果推广到Higgs丛模空间及(A,A,A)和(A,B,A)Brane的拓扑研究。

Conclusion: 揭示了实向量丛模空间连通分支数与基曲线实点存在性、秩与度的互素性之间的深层联系，并将这些拓扑结果推广至Higgs丛模空间及超凯勒商中的Brane分类。

Abstract: Let $X$ be a Riemann surface of genus $g \geqslant 2$ and let $σ: X \to X$ be an antiholomorphic involution on $X$. Let $\mathcal{N}(r,d)$ be the moduli space of semistable vector bundles of rank $r$ and degree $d$ on $X$, with the induced real structure. Using a gauge-theoretic approach, we determine the number of connected components of the real locus of $\mathcal{N}(r,d)$ for general $r$ and $d$. We show in particular that, when the base curve has real points, quaternionic vector bundles can exist for even rank and degree but that the number of connected components of $\mathbb{R}\mathcal{N}(r,d)$ is still equal to that of $\mathbb{R}\mathrm{Pic}_d$. In contrast, when the base curve has empty real locus and $r$ and $d$ are not coprime, the number of connected components of $\mathbb{R}\mathcal{N}(r,d)$ can be smaller than that of $\mathbb{R}\mathrm{Pic}_d$. We then generalize these results to real loci of moduli spaces of Higgs bundles and apply them to the study of the topology of certain $(A,A,A)$ and $(A,B,A)$ branes in the associated hyperkähler quotient.

</details>


### [193] [Graded Keller maps and the Jacobian Conjecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20210)
*T. Shaska*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文通过加权投影空间的稀疏有理点视角分析Jacobian猜想，证明了正权重条件下等变Keller映射必为自同构（无反例），而最近提出的反例在权重符号混合时其像集为稀疏集，且Kummer条件在堆栈层上重现，提出了按权重符号分类等变多项式映射的框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将加权投影空间上有理点的稀疏性结果（arXiv:2509.02319）应用于Jacobian猜想，探讨权重符号模式对等变多项式映射性质的决定性作用，并解释最近提出的反例为何能绕过正权重情形下的障碍。

Method: 分析Veronese态射下有理点提升的Kummer条件，将等变Keller映射按权重符号分类（全正、混合符号）；通过降维到商空间，将Keller条件转化为商映射Jacobian沿收缩轨迹的消没阶条件；利用堆栈层上的平方根条件（Kummer条件）解释反例的理性点存在性。

Result: 在正权重（加权投影空间）情形下，等变Keller映射必为自同构，无反例；在二维情形下，任何符号模式均成立。反例的像在ℚ上为稀疏集，且沿μ₂稳定子线，两个原像在-a为平方数时均为有理点，重现了正权重理论中的Kummer条件。

Conclusion: 提出了按权重符号签名分类等变多项式映射的方案，其中全正权重情形对应加权投影几何，是"良好"情形；混合符号情形则允许反例存在，且涉及更微妙的数论条件。

Abstract: Rational points on weighted projective spaces are sparse: a point of $\mathbb{P}^n(\mathbb{Q})$ lifts along the Veronese morphism only when a Kummer condition holds at every prime (arXiv:2509.02319). We ask what this viewpoint says about the Jacobian Conjecture. The map recently announced as a counterexample is equivariant for the grading $\mathrm{wt}(x,y,z)=(1,-1,-2)$, and we show that the sign pattern of such a grading decides everything. If the weights are all positive, the setting of weighted projective spaces, an equivariant Keller map is always an automorphism, so no counterexample can be graded that way. In dimension two the same holds for every sign pattern. The Keller condition itself descends to the quotient, where it says that the Jacobian of the quotient map vanishes to order two along the contracted locus. Over $\mathbb{Q}$ the image of the counterexample is a thin set. But along the line where the group action has stabilizer $μ_2$, the two preimages on the contracted locus are rational exactly when $-a$ is a square, so the Kummer condition of the positive-weight theory reappears on the stacky stratum. We propose a classification of equivariant polynomial maps by the signature of the weights, with weighted projective geometry as the positive case.

</details>


### [194] [On the global and local geometry of quasi-$F$-split varieties with trivial canonical bundle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20272)
*Jefferson Baudin*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有平凡典范丛的拟F-分裂簇的几何与奇点性质，包括：证明正则拟F^∞-分裂簇非几何无理性且具有几何典范奇点；构造了非拟F^∞-分裂的拟F-分裂曲面（反驳了Kawakami等人的问题）；证明正规拟F-分裂簇的几何正规性；以及在奇异解消假设下证明拟F^e-纯簇的对数典范性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决与具有平凡典范丛的拟F-分裂簇相关的几何与奇点问题，包括推广先前结果、回答公开问题以及建立新的奇点性质。

Method: 通过代数几何和正特征代数几何的方法，包括F-分裂理论、奇异解消假设、反例构造等。

Result: (1) 正则拟F^∞-分裂簇非几何无理性且具有几何典范奇点；(2) 存在非拟F^∞-分裂的拟F-分裂曲面；(3) 正规拟F-分裂簇是几何正规的；(4) 在奇异解消假设下，满足特定条件的拟F^e-纯簇是对数典范的。

Conclusion: 本文推广了Patakfalvi和Zdanowicz的结果，否定了Kawakami等人的问题，扩展了Kawakami等人的几何正规性结果，并建立了拟F^e-纯簇的对数典范性。

Abstract: We solve certain questions related to the geometry and singularities of quasi-$F$-split varieties with trivial canonical bundle. First, we prove that regular quasi-$F^{\infty}$-split varieties are not geometrically uniruled (this generalizes and significantly simplifies the earlier results of Patakfalvi and Zdanowicz) and have geometrically canonical singularities. Second, we show that there exist quasi-$F$-split surfaces with trivial canonical bundle which are not quasi-$F^{\infty}$-split, answering negatively a question raised by Kawakami, Takamatsu, Tanaka, Witaszek, Yobuko and Yoshikawa. Third, we show that normal quasi-$F$-split varieties with trivial canonical bundle are geometrically normal (this extends a result of Kawakami, Takamatsu and Yoshikawa), and finally we prove that quasi-$F^e$-pure normal varieties $X$ such that $mp^eK_X$ is Cartier for $m$ coprime to $p$ are log canonical, under a resolution of singularities hypothesis.

</details>

Result: 得到了复杂半阿贝尔簇在任意维度下的有效特征描述，并验证了所设假设的紧致性（sharpness）。

### [196] [Automorphism groups of curves with simple Jacobians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20397)
*Luca Mauri*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文分类了特征为0的代数闭域上所有具单色雅克比的光滑射影连通曲线的自同构群，并为每个非平凡群构造了曲线族，证明密度为1的成员具有单色雅克比，且这些族在主极化阿贝尔簇模空间中产生了无限多个新的"不可能相交"例子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过对所有自同构群的完整分类，结合构造特定曲线族和密度论证（证明成员具有单色雅克比的比例为1）来实现目标。

Result: 完成了所有满足条件的曲线的自同构群分类，并为每个非平凡自同构群构造了曲线族，这些族中几乎所有成员都具有单色雅克比。

Abstract: We classify all automorphism groups of smooth, projective, connected curves over an algebraically closed field of characteristic $0$ with simple Jacobians. For every nontrivial group in this classification, we construct a family of curves with that automorphism group and prove that a density-one set of members has simple Jacobian. These families yield infinitely many new examples of unlikely intersections in the moduli spaces of principally polarized abelian varieties.
